Disarmament Convention Begins Organization 28

Drafting Committee Uses British and American Plans to Draft Convention Text

Ignores Japan's Proposal to Negotiate New Naval Agreement

Adjourns for Four Weeks After First Reading

(Geneva) The Main Committee today decided to ask the Drafting Committee to begin drafting a new draft of the disarmament convention based on the proposals made by the British representative, hoping that the General Committee can approve its method of proceeding. The current plan is for the Drafting Committee to draft the convention text based on the British and American proposals, completely ignoring Japan's proposal to allow the negotiation of a new naval agreement. Judging from the resolution of the Main Committee, it is evident that Britain, the United States, France, and Italy have no intention of reintroducing the naval issue at this time. The new draft convention is expected to be drafted within a few days and will be submitted to the General Committee for a first reading. The amendments agreed upon during the first reading will then be submitted to the Drafting Committee for revision, and the General Committee will adjourn until June 27, so that the initial efforts of the World Economic Conference can be entirely limited to economic matters and not be distracted by other affairs. Some disarmament representatives may also attend the London Conference. At that time, the Drafting Committee will remain in Geneva to continue drafting. The General Committee has already voted on the adjournment and authorized Chairman Henderson to adjourn for three weeks or more if he deems it necessary. However, the General Committee has not yet made a decision on the request of the Main Committee to provide concrete instructions on the adoption of the British plan. Although the United States has fully endorsed the British plan, except for a few points, and France has also accepted the British plan as a basis for discussion, it is anticipated that the General Committee will approve the request of the Main Committee. Some drafting committee members are quite concerned that the new draft convention may not be completed until June 9, but the members will work hard to expedite its completion. The key points of the British plan are threefold: to stipulate the agreed-upon actual number of European land forces, to conclude a consultation convention, and to reaffirm the provisions of the Washington and London naval treaties. Although Japan generally agrees, it wants to avoid mentioning the existing naval treaties altogether.

Disarmament Conference Decides to Adjourn Until July 3 29

(Geneva) The General Committee of the Disarmament Conference decided this afternoon to adjourn immediately after the first reading of the draft convention submitted by Britain. The resumption of the meeting is scheduled to be no later than July 3. The first reading of the British draft is expected to be completed on Saturday. As for the decision of the Main Committee yesterday to draft a new draft convention based on the British plan, due to the opposition of the representatives of France, Norway, and Switzerland, it was decided that the General Committee would not make this proposal until the first reading of the British draft was completed. However, the Disarmament Conference will not completely waste time during the adjournment period, as the General Committee has adopted the compromise proposal of the American representative, Hugh Wilson. Therefore, the Main Committee will continue to meet from time to time, and Chairman Henderson will conduct separate consultations in order to draft a new draft convention. The General Committee met at 11:00 this morning, but immediately after the meeting began, someone opposed the decision of the Main Committee yesterday. French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour and Norwegian representative Lange both opposed adopting the British draft as the basis for a future international convention before the first reading of the British draft was completed. The representatives of Yugoslavia, Turkey, the Netherlands, and Persia opposed the Main Committee's proposal to engage in consultations and draft a new convention during the adjournment period, arguing that limiting the number of committee members to a few major powers was unfair. Then, the French representative attacked the Main Committee's proposal from another angle, insisting that the chapters on prohibiting private manufacturing of munitions and limiting military budgets should also be included in the new convention. Thereupon, Chairman Henderson attempted to quell the opposition of the small countries and proposed that he be authorized to consult on the new convention during the adjournment period, and proposed extending the adjournment period, moving its termination date from June 27 to July 2. The representatives of Yugoslavia, the Netherlands, and Turkey all agreed. The General Committee made the aforementioned decision at 2:00 PM, then took a short break and scheduled to reconvene at 3:00 PM to continue the first reading of the chapter on supervision of disarmament in the British draft. It is expected that the French representative will submit many amendments to strengthen the power of the provisions at that time. (Kokumin dispatch, 1st)

American Delegation Heads to England 33

Attending the World Economic Conference

Roosevelt Changes Procedures for Resolving War Debts

To Proceed Through Normal Diplomatic Channels

(Washington) The American delegation to the Economic Conference, Secretary of State Hull, economic elder statesman Cox, Senator Pittman, Representative McReynolds, accompanied by 15 aides, set sail for London today. Senator Costigan and other representatives will depart within the next week. The US government finally added Morrison, a retired banker from San Antonio, as a representative, who also traveled today. Before his departure, Hull claimed that the American delegation would first focus on reducing tariffs, stabilizing exchange rates, and raising prices, but he declined to disclose the details of his plan, saying only that he believed that after talks between the president and politicians from various countries, the major issues at the conference could be agreed upon within three weeks. (Kokumin dispatch, 31st)

(Washington) The White House announced today that the US President has completely changed the procedure for resolving war debts, no longer entrusting it to Secretary of State Hull or other representatives to negotiate outside the London Conference, but instead being personally presided over by the President and continuing negotiations through normal diplomatic channels. This is because the President feels that if war debt negotiations are conducted concurrently with the Economic Conference, it will distract the representatives and prevent them from concentrating their attention. He also feels that after talks with politicians from various countries in Washington, all parties have a clear understanding of the issues and believes that the war debt issue can now be addressed on the basis of this understanding. (Kokumin dispatch, 31st)

Germany Addresses Unemployment 60

To Issue Bonds Worth 1 Billion Marks

To Promote Industry and Initiate Projects

Reuter, Berlin, 31st – A proposal to authorize the Ministry of Finance to issue bonds worth one billion marks, enabling the government to implement its unemployment relief plan, was passed by the Cabinet today. This plan was initiated by the President of the German National Bank, Schacht, who will oversee its financial aspects. The plan includes projects such as repairing public and private buildings, developing suburban garden cities and rural areas, and constructing new national roads. The plan also has other distinctive features: (1) a provision for women to leave employment and return to household duties; (2) encouraging marriage, with financial assistance for families; and (3) promoting industry and increasing production to counter dumping by countries with devalued currencies.

International Chamber of Commerce Congress 61

Havas, Vienna, 31st – The International Chamber of Commerce Congress convened here today, passing two resolutions. One advocated continued international negotiations to abolish double taxation. The second called for the abolition of currency controls in the short term. At the third session, the issue of currency stabilization was discussed. The French representative, Song Li, strongly criticized the harm caused by currency fluctuations, stating that silver could not serve as a standard for trade between nations and that the gold standard should be restored. The Italian representative, Bian Zhini, said that he had previously advocated organizing a public fund to achieve currency stabilization. Another Italian representative, Pi Lai Li, said that the universal support of the congress delegates for removing currency barriers was very gratifying. The American representative, Wadsworth, believed that the main cause of the global economic crisis was the excessive increase in the budgets of most countries.

Nazi Party Headquarters Raided 62

Restrictions on German Goods Imports

Reuter, Vienna, 31st – Police today raided the headquarters of the National Socialist Party here, as well as the residences of Nazi leaders in Vienna and other locations, including the residence of Habicht, Hitler's commissioner in Austria. Habicht is currently negotiating with Austrian Chancellor Dr. Dollfuss on the merger of the Nazi Party and the Christian Social Party (the ruling party). Today, Habicht declared that negotiations had failed because the Austrian government was unwilling to allow the Nazi Party to participate in the cabinet according to its strength.

National News Agency, Vienna, 31st – The Austrian government has now ordered Austrians wishing to go to Germany to obtain passports. The German government stipulates that Germans going to Austria must pay 1,000 marks for a passport fee, while the Austrian government only charges a fee for issuing passports, thereby monitoring the movement of people between the two countries. The Austrian government has also decided to compensate hotels for financial losses incurred due to the new German regulations, amounting to approximately 10 million Austrian schillings. The Austrian government has also restricted the import of German goods, ensuring that their total value does not exceed Austrian exports to Germany. This measure will harm Germany, as Germany has traditionally had a trade surplus with Austria. In the past five years, Germany's sales to Austria have exceeded Austria's sales to Germany by more than 1,200,000,000 Austrian schillings.

Stimson Agrees to French and German Request to Chair Conciliation Committee 63

Havas, Paris, 31st – The Locarno Accords of 1925 include an arbitration treaty between France and Germany. This treaty stipulates the establishment of a permanent conciliation committee. The French and German governments have agreed to appoint former U.S. Secretary of State Stimson as chairman, and this has been formally announced.

Anhui's New Chairman, Liu Zhenhua, Takes Office 64

Announces Governance Policies for Anhui Upon Taking Office

Overview of Financial Management Over the Past Year

Anqing Correspondence – The newly appointed Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, Liu Zhenhua, along with the Director of Civil Affairs, Ma Lingfu, the Director of Finance, Mao Longzhang, and the Director of Education, Yang Lian, arrived in Anhui on the Changxing vessel of the Sanbei Company at 6:00 AM on the 29th. In anticipation, officials and members of the political circles, as well as the provincial government military band and police personnel, all gathered at the Sanbei Wharf to await their arrival. The Highway Bureau also dispatched several vehicles to welcome them. (The road from the provincial government to the Sanbei Wharf had recently been completed overnight and a completion ceremony was held in front of the provincial government at 4:30 PM on the 28th, followed by a test drive.) After disembarking, Liu shook hands with the welcoming party and entered the city by car, heading directly to the provincial government to rest. Li Yingsheng, a member of the Provincial Committee, and Liu Yiyan, a member of the Provincial Committee and Director of Construction, had already arrived in the province beforehand. The remaining member of the Provincial Committee, Ye Yuanlong, who also serves as Secretary-General, Hu Rulin, still needs to arrive. Liu was originally scheduled to take office on June 1st, but because he also serves as the Commander-in-Chief of the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Area Bandit Suppression, he urgently needed to take office. Therefore, the ceremony was rescheduled for 10:00 AM on the 30th in the auditorium of the provincial government. Over a thousand representatives from various circles and officials from various institutions attended. The ceremony was conducted according to protocol. First, Liu delivered a report and announced his governance policies for Anhui, including (1) purifying officialdom, (2) rectifying education, (3) making finances transparent, and (4) providing relief to rural areas. Then, Wu Rencang, a member of the Anhui Provincial Party Rectification Committee, delivered a speech. After the speeches, a group photo was taken and the ceremony concluded. Subsequently, Liu and the directors of the various departments began their duties.

Another report states that Anhui Province's tax revenue, before the abolition of the Likin tax, was over 11 million yuan per year for both national and local taxes. After the abolition of the Likin tax, it was only over 9 million yuan. In 1919, expenditures increased sharply, and revenue and expenditure could not be balanced. The budget for the 21st year was reduced from over 13 million yuan to over 11 million yuan, which could still balance revenue and expenditure. Before April 20th of last year, various institutions were in arrears of funds, with some owing up to five months. The accumulated arrears of regular expenses totaled over 797,000 yuan, and the accumulated arrears of temporary expenses totaled over 4.267 million yuan, for a total of over 3.94 million yuan. This did not include the 500,000 yuan of treasury bills issued. After Wu Zhongxin took charge of Anhui, through more than a year of patching up, the current arrears of regular expenses are only over 370,000 yuan, and the arrears of temporary expenses are only over 410,000 yuan. The unappropriated funds are also only 1.44 million yuan, for a total of over 1.7 million yuan that has been paid back. 250,000 yuan of treasury bills have also been cashed. The field tax for the 21st year was pre-allocated by Chen Tiaoyuan during his tenure, amounting to around one million yuan. The field tax for the 22nd year has not yet been used. Now that Liu Zhenhua has succeeded as the head of Anhui's administration and has expressed that finances will be transparent, if he continues to rectify the situation, it may not be difficult to balance revenue and expenditure in a year's time. (May 31st)

Third Sheet

Sino-Japanese Armistice Negotiations Begin 65

Chinese and Japanese Representatives Gather in Tanggu

Three Japanese Warships Anchor Offshore

Situation of Japanese Troops in the Withdrawal Zone

No Complications Expected in the Future

Special Dispatch from Beiping – Since the practical methods for a cease-fire were agreed upon, Sino-Japanese peace negotiations have been actively underway. After several days of consultation between the two sides, the negotiation location and the number of representatives have been completely determined. Each side has sent six representatives to Tanggu, a more suitable location, to hold negotiations. After careful selection for several days, our side has decided on Xiong Bin, Zhang Qun, He Zhuguo, Yin Rugeng, Liu Ximing, and Zhang Shouguang as the six representatives, representing various relevant parties and responsible for coordination. Xiong Bin will serve as the chief representative. In addition to the representatives, Qian Zongze, Xu Zuyi, and several others have been hired as specialized committee members for the purpose of gathering ideas from various sources. The Japanese representatives are the Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army, Koiso, the Deputy Chief of Staff, Okamura, the Commander of the Tianjin Garrison Army, Nakamura, the military representative, Major General Tani, the military attache, Colonel Nagasawa, and the secretary of the Japanese Embassy, Tanaka. Koiso and Okamura, along with their entourage, arrived in Tanggu yesterday (29th) afternoon at 5:00 PM aboard the Japanese warship and entered the Japanese barracks after landing. Nagasawa has been in Beiping for a long time, and Tani also arrived in Beiping yesterday morning to make contact. This morning, Tani, Nagasawa, and Tanaka, the three representatives, went to Tanggu on a special train with our representatives. Nakamura also went from Tianjin. After our representatives were determined, the Railway Bureau prepared a special train yesterday afternoon and parked it at Yongdingmen. This morning (30th) at around 7:00 AM, Xiong Bin, Zhang Qun, Qian Zongze, Xu Zuyi, and the Japanese representatives Tani, Nagasawa, and Tanaka successively arrived at the Yongdingmen station to board the train. Security was extremely tight at the platform. The train departed at 7:55 AM, with two rows of military police on board to provide protection. Before the train departed, an armored train left from the East Station to clear the tracks. At 10:40 AM, the special train arrived in Tianjin. He Zhuguo, Liu Ximing, Yin Rugeng, and Zhang Daoguang boarded the train to travel together. At around 12:00 PM, they left Tianjin heading east and arrived in Tanggu at 2:00 PM. Representatives' residences and conference venue in Tanggu had been prepared in advance. The conference venue was decided to be in the China Merchants Bureau conference hall. After the representatives from both sides gathered in Tanggu, they will first engage in informal socializing, meeting each other. Formal negotiations are scheduled to begin tomorrow (31st). Due to the Boxer Protocol, a small team of Japanese soldiers was originally stationed in Tanggu. With the arrival of the Japanese representatives for the conference, the number of soldiers has been slightly increased. Yesterday, two Japanese warships arrived in Tanggu, and this morning (30th) at 6:30 AM, another warship arrived, carrying three 5-inch guns. There are now three Japanese warships anchored in the waters off Tanggu, seemingly displaying military force at sea to protect their peace representatives. Although there have been informal contacts regarding various issues beforehand, there are still various difficult problems obstructing progress. Whether or not things will proceed smoothly in the future will depend on the sincerity of the Japanese side. However, in general, there is optimism regarding the future of the negotiations, and it is believed that no complications will arise midway.

The front lines have been generally quiet in recent days, but the puppet troops are still very active, with minor disputes occurring. The Japanese troops claim to be unaware, which is likely deliberate. Since yesterday, Tongzhou, Shunyi, and other places have been extremely peaceful. Near Lutai, in the Tianzhuangtai area, the puppet troops and the volunteer army of Zheng Guilin's unit had a small conflict. Tianzhuangtai was occupied by the puppet troops yesterday morning. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Zheng Guilin led his guards in a counterattack, crossing the north bank from Erdaoqiao and occupying Peijiazhuang. They are currently confronting the enemy at Liu Da Gongzhuang. The wounded soldiers of Zheng's unit were transported to Beiping for treatment this morning. In the Ninghe area, the puppet troops of Zhao Lei's unit are still occupying the city. Japanese troops in Hedong are at Yangzhuangzi, occasionally firing at our Mengzhuang position. Our troops are maintaining calm. North of Luofa on the Pingjin Line, Japanese scouting soldiers were previously discovered but have now retreated, and the area is peaceful. This morning, a Japanese plane flew to Tongzhou for reconnaissance, and two planes also flew to the Gaoliying area of Changping, purely to scout our movements. As for the skies over Beiping, no Japanese planes have been seen for several days.

Another special report states that the Chinese and Japanese armies have entered a state of ceasefire since the two sides began armistice negotiations. In the Ninghe area, the Mori Regiment of Japanese cavalry had retreated to the area of Lihuamaozhuang, Dayuzhuang, and Yangbozhuang by 1:00 AM last night (29th). Most of the Japanese troops are still confronting our troops on the line from the west gate of Ninghe to Renhanzhuang. In Xianghe, most of the Japanese troops are gathered in the city, and all city gates are tightly closed and not opened, prohibiting people from entering and exiting. Japanese infantry and cavalry, numbering about 500, are also stationed in Ma, Fang, Xiejialou, Dadong and other villages. The Japanese troops in Wuqing previously sent puppet troops to organize plainclothes teams, hoping to cross the river from Luofa and disturb our rear, but they did not succeed due to strict precautions. In other areas, such as the Lutai area on the Beining Line, although there are occasional disturbances by puppet troops, no fierce battles have occurred in recent days. The Japanese troops on the Pinggu Avenue have withdrawn towards Miyun, but their artillery is still at Shilipu and has not moved. At around 10:00 AM today (30th) in Tongzhou, a Japanese plane flew over for reconnaissance, circling for a long time before flying northeast. At 10:10 AM in Gaoliying, two Japanese planes flew from Changping, circled several times, and flew south. At around 3:00 PM on the 29th, four or five Japanese scouts were discovered in the Beiwulibanqiao area and quickly left. Japanese cavalry occasionally go to the vicinity of our defense zone to patrol and scout. The Japanese scouting soldiers in the Luofa area have already left. The situation in Shunyi has not changed. The situation on all lines is generally very calm. At present, all parties are focusing their attention on the issue of peace and are paying close attention to the progress of the armistice negotiations. The scope of these armistice negotiations is limited to military affairs. The party in charge of everything on the Japanese side is the Kwantung Army Headquarters. Previously, Nakayama, the acting representative of the Japanese Embassy in Beiping, and Nakamura, the commander of the Japanese army in Tianjin, telegraphed Araki, requesting instructions on the armistice issue. After Araki replied to the Kwantung Army Commander Kobuto, seeking his consent, preliminary verbal consultations began. Therefore, Koiso is also traveling with them this time. It is expected that the issue of the demilitarized zone and the disposition of the Northeast volunteer army will be discussed during the meeting. The Japanese army has proposed that neither side station troops within 24 miles inside the Great Wall. This may be raised again after the meeting is held, but because it is purely a local problem and does not include political or diplomatic issues, it is expected that opinions will be easier to reconcile before the meeting. (Dispatch from May 30th)

A Visit to the Guangxi Reclamation and Water Conservancy Experimental Area (Continued) 67

(IV) Work Achievements Over the Past Year

The area has been in operation for exactly one year now. Looking back on this year, we want to know if there have been any significant achievements, and what those achievements are. Now I will briefly describe the achievements of the area in the past year. (1) The Lending Office When the Lending Office was first established, farmers were generally in a state of fear due to long-term oppression and exploitation by landlords. When the area sent people to the countryside to promote lending in mid-March, farmers thought it was just another trick by the government or a vicious harmful policy, and they all dared not try it. The propagandists wanted them to sign a letter of intent, but they absolutely refused. Later, unintentionally, several workers who were working in the area short-term needed money and borrowed from the Lending Office. The Lending Office lent them money according to the procedures, at an interest rate of 1%, and this incident opened the door. Farmers began to believe in the Lending Office. Within ten days, hundreds of farmers came to request loans, some borrowing 100 yuan, some borrowing 50 yuan, and some borrowing 30 yuan. Within just ten days, 30,000 yuan had already been lent out. From this, we can see how deeply farmers are oppressed by usury and local forces, and how urgent the need for low-interest loans is in rural areas. When farmers borrow money from the Lending Office, they must first undergo an investigation to determine their degree of need and whether the purpose is legitimate, and then determine the amount of the loan. The repayment period is after the autumn harvest. Farmers have excellent credit, and 95% of them repay the full amount before the deadline, and 5% repay on time. When the reporter went to visit, the third phase of loans was being issued. The lending office was filled with farmers, all looking happy and joyful. The staff at the office are very serious about their work. Farmers borrowing money must first be interviewed in person by the director of the Economic Improvement Organization, who determines the amount and other factors face to face. Usually, the director carries a small bag on his back and goes to the countryside to investigate, sleeping in farmhouses at night, never complaining. The director studied in Japan and is a passionate practitioner. In addition, the Lending Office's warehouse is under construction and will be completed soon. Farmers will be able to use the warehouse to store grain during this fall harvest.

(2) Reclamation A central farm and a horticulture farm have been established in Shatang, with an area of only 1,000 mu. 3,000 mu have been reclaimed in the Shibeiping area. Recently, eight gasoline plowing machines are being used to reclaim land, and it will soon reach over 10,000 mu. In the Wuyou area, about 1,000 mu of paddy fields have been reclaimed. In total, about 5,000 mu of wasteland has been reclaimed in the area in the past year, excluding afforestation, which is less than one-twentieth of the planned reclamation area. In the future, reclamation and planting will be intensified.

(3) Water Conservancy The area has a very large plan for water conservancy. The rivers in Guangxi mostly have rocky beds and very turbulent water flows. If a little artificial work is added, they can be utilized. Most people are not easy to convince, so the area is currently starting to utilize hydropower facilities. The plan is to build dams on the rivers to raise the water level, and then use the water force to install motors. The area is paying attention to the preliminary scale of this matter, and there are already some clues. If the plan is realized, it will not only drastically develop rural production, but also open a new era for the industrialization of agriculture in Guangxi. Its future is truly unlimited.

(4) Transportation Developed rural production requires convenient transportation. The area has paid attention to this point early on. About 70 li of automobile roads and 50 li of field roads have already been built, greatly increasing transportation convenience. In addition, the Liucheng waterway is also sufficient to aid transportation.

(5) Surveying The area has a surveying training class, which is used for its own purposes and is often hired by other counties.

(6) Investigation Rural investigation is extremely important in rural construction, because all facilities must be based on precise investigation, otherwise they will be empty and unsupported. However, at the same time, rural investigation is also one of the most difficult tasks. Investigators often do not fulfill their duties and arbitrarily fabricate reports, often causing the entire investigation to be useless. I remember a certain province's Department of Agriculture and Mines conducting a rural investigation. After the investigators arrived in various counties, they only sat in the county seat, and sent official letters in the form of detention orders to summon the village chiefs of various villages, briefly asked them questions according to the form, and then considered it done. Although our country has recently gradually realized the importance of statistics, major domestic agencies have mostly set up statistics departments to specialize in this matter, but in practice, they are nothing more than the situations described above, or they pass through official documents, from the National Government to the Provincial Government to the County Government, and the county then passes it down to the district office, and the district then passes it down to the township head. If the township head has nowhere to transfer it, they then rely on what their minds can imagine, filling it in arbitrarily. Some even do it because the deadline is approaching, and the county does not pass it down to the district, but a few clerks who only know "due to the reasons mentioned above, I am writing this" vaguely fill it in, and then consider it done. These statistics are naturally completely unreliable. The area's investigations are not perfect because it lacks investigators who are fully trained to specialize in this matter, but because of its frequent contact with farmers through loans, it is relatively reliable. Half of it is also due to the seriousness of the area's staff in their work, so it has achieved relatively significant results.

In conclusion, it is still too early to say whether the area's business operations will be realized as expected in the future, and even if they are realized, whether they can solve the entire rural problem of China. However, speaking only of the pilot area itself, with its perfect plan, noble purpose, and the efforts of its staff, it is certain that it will have a considerable development in the future. This is something that we can predict.

General Headquarters Orders Hubei Provincial Government to Cooperate with Military in Suppressing Bandits 69

Orders Counties with Dikes to Strictly Prevent Floods in Accordance with Regulations

Chief of Staff of 51st Division Ding Teng Accused of Profiteering and Dies Under Prosecution

Hankou Correspondence: The General Headquarters of Bandit Suppression in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, believing that the remaining bandits in Hubei have not yet been eliminated, and that the county magistrates of various counties have failed to cooperate with the military, and that the members of the local defense forces are complex and poorly trained, is an important reason. On the 30th, it strictly ordered the Hubei Provincial Government, as well as the Department of Civil Affairs, the Security Office, the Administrative Commissioners, and the county magistrates of various counties that if they procrastinate again, they will be removed and punished. The order said: "The suppression of the remaining bandits requires the cooperation of the local administrative officials and the suppression forces. It also relies on the organization of local security teams to be properly organized and to strengthen the self-defense capabilities of the people in order to be effective. Recently, reports have stated that bandits lurking in central and western Hubei have not been eliminated, all because the county magistrates of various counties have failed to do their best to cooperate as the main reason. Especially, the security teams are not well organized, the members are complex, the system is unclear, and they have failed to take consistent actions with the military, which often leads to missed opportunities, which has allowed the bandit forces to spread, which cannot be denied. The county magistrates of various counties have the responsibility of the local area and should deeply understand their duties and eliminate evil without reservation, in order to achieve a permanent solution. If the remaining bandits are not eliminated for one day, the duties are not fulfilled for one day. After this order is issued, if they still procrastinate, neglect their duties, fail to assist with efforts, or fail to effectively organize security teams, the provincial government, the Department of Civil Affairs, and the Security Office shall investigate and remove and punish them. During the period of suppression, the security teams of various counties shall also follow the organizational regulations of the Administrative Commissioners' Offices and be subject to the command of the senior generals of the bandit suppression in order to achieve unified effectiveness."

(Flood Prevention of the Jianghan Main Dike)

On the 30th, the General Headquarters issued an order to the counties along the Jianghan Dike to strictly prevent floods in accordance with the regulations. The order said: "The Secretariat of this Headquarters presented a case and approved a letter from the National Economic Council, stating that the Jianghan industry in Hubei Province flows through dozens of counties, and building dikes to control water is extremely important. Between summer and autumn, floods rise, and the long dikes of thousands of miles are in danger inch by inch. Defense and rescue are especially urgent. The key to safety lies in whether laborers and materials can be rushed to work in a hurry. Therefore, it is necessary to inspect dangerous areas in advance and prepare materials. It is especially necessary to summon laborers and supervise them to work in order to avoid delaying the opportunity. Therefore, the local government must be responsible for handling flood prevention matters in the past, so that the collection of materials and laborers can be done locally. The major annual maintenance projects of the Jianghan Main Dike in Hubei Province have been strictly ordered by this council to the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to speed up the work and will be gradually completed. Now that the flood season is approaching, the flood prevention matters of the Jianghan Main Dike should be decided as soon as possible, and the local government should still be responsible for the preparations in order to avoid negligence. Now, according to the situation of the Jianghan Main Dike and referring to the annual maintenance regulations, thirteen articles of the flood prevention measures for the Jianghan Main Dike this year have been drafted. A letter is sent accordingly, hoping that you will investigate and forward it to the approval, and instruct the relevant local governments of the Jianghan Main Dike to comply with the regulations. The matter concerns the dike, so be careful not to delay and neglect. You should also report the compliance to this Headquarters for verification."

(Corrupt Military Officials Should Be Brought to Justice)

Ding Teng, Chief of Staff of the 51st Division and Chief of Staff of the Xiangfan Garrison Headquarters, was accused of profiteering and harming the people. A total of more than 170 cocoon shops in the four townships reported to be opening. Yesterday (1st) was the first day of the cocoon shops opening. Weng Zhendong, a wealthy household in Xuedian Township, 12th District of the county, was kidnapped by a bandit gang and extorted a huge sum of money last winter. Zhu Meiji, the chief of the 8th District, captured the main culprits in this case, Huang Baojin, Chen Zengbao, and six others, and one accomplice and sent them to court. In addition to Huang Baojin and Chen Zengbao, who were interrogated by the county government and executed by firing squad in accordance with the Law on Punishing Bandits, the remaining five were transferred to the court for interrogation. Now it is learned that the case has been investigated and prosecuted by the court clearly. After interrogating the criminals yesterday, the sentences were immediately announced. Fang Laifu, Xu Yuanchi, and Zou Ashi were sentenced to death, Zhuang Shigen was sentenced to life imprisonment, and Shi Rengen was found to be unrelated and was acquitted.

Robbery of Farmers in the 11th District 73

Qian Renbao's family, a farmer in Weitianwan near Hongshengli, 11th District of the county, was suddenly visited by more than ten bandits at about 1:00 a.m. the night before, carrying iron rulers, sharp blades, and wooden sticks. They kicked open the back door and swarmed in, tying up Renbao's daughter-in-law and her young grandson Ar Xiao with ropes, threatening and beating them. Then they searched everywhere and carried away the stolen goods after an hour. After the incident, the lost items were counted, and the loss was about more than 100 yuan. They have come to the city to report the case and request the arrest.

Tragedy of Arson at the Door 74

Leng Agou, a Jiangxi native, runs a bamboo shop in the East Street of Taixiang Town, 15th District of the county, with two apprentices, one twenty years old and one only twelve. However, in the past six months, he has suddenly been angered by his enemies. From time to time, someone poured flammable kerosene, etc. on the buckets to set fire. As for the reason, it is said that it was a plot by fellow villagers, or envy. The situation is complicated and difficult to speculate. After 2:00 a.m. yesterday morning, a fire suddenly broke out again at the door of Leng's shop. The fire was fierce and there was no back door. One of the ten-year-old apprentices was actually engulfed in the fire. Leng and the twelve-year-old apprentice escaped from the raging fire during sleep, suffering severe burns. The man hired a boat and took them to the city for medical treatment, but as soon as the boat arrived at the dock, the twelve-year-old apprentice had died of his injuries. Fearing that they would be summoned by the officials, the carriers took the teacher and apprentice, one alive and one dead, back to their hometown to take care of them.

Changzhou County Government Executes Five Bandits by Firing Squad

The Zoumatang Security Group in the 9th District of Wu邑武邑captured five bandits, Hou Bingli, Yang Changen, Yang Genfa, Jin Renquan, and Guan Arda, etc. in Pangjia Street, and seized many items such as rifles, bullets, and stolen goods. After being sent to the county for interrogation, they confessed to repeatedly committing crimes and burning the victims without hesitation. It was proposed to sentence them to death and reported to the provincial government. In the afternoon of May 31, County Magistrate Cai received a telegram from the provincial government, approving the execution of the five criminals, Hou Bingli, etc. by firing squad. He immediately signed the order to bring the criminals to justice, verify their identities, and send a team to escort them to the Fengweidun execution ground for execution by firing squad.

Jiangyin Nine-Year-Old Boy Goes to Study in Switzerland

In Geneva, Switzerland, children from all countries who are eight years old are eligible to enroll in school. My country has never had a place. This spring, Li Shizeng, the president of the Peking Research Institute, discussed with the chairman of the school board, the Director of Health of the League of Nations, Mr. Lachsman, and obtained six places, two for overseas Chinese and two each for the north and south. One is the young son of Zhang Gongquan, the president of the Bank of China in Shanghai, and the other is Hu Xiangxiong, the young son of Hu Yunge in Jiangyin, who is only nine years old. Hu is a top student in Zhongjie Primary School. Recently, he received a quick mail from Li Shizeng, urging Hu to go to Shanghai this week, and Li will escort him on a ship to go abroad. Yesterday (30th), the entire faculty and students of the school held a farewell party and presented a large silver seat as a souvenir. Today (31st), Hu Xiangxiong was accompanied by his father to Shanghai to wait for the ship to go abroad.

Cantonese Arrested for Gambling in Qingyang 75

A large number of Cantonese arrived in Qingyang Township, Beixiang a few days ago and planned to organize a large-scale gambling den there. Yesterday (30th), Wu Bingjun, the director of the Second Public Security Bureau, led the police to arrest nine people, including Yi Cai, and immediately sent them to the General Bureau to be transferred to the county for review.

Nantong Crazy Man Tragically Kills Brother

Wu Xiaodaoshi, a villager in Houyouzha, Jinle District, Nantong, who is 61 years old this year, asked his 64-year-old brother, Wu Changdang, to come to his home to help cut wheat. He stayed overnight that night. At dawn, he suddenly killed his brother with a kitchen knife and dismembered him into three sections. While he was skinning him, he was surrounded and arrested by neighbors and sent to the Public Security Bureau to be transferred to the court. The neighbors Xing Wangshun, etc. were summoned for questioning. Wu Xiaodaoshi has been suffering from madness for more than ten years. He has been living alone. This time, he asked Shi to cut wheat, but it turned into a tragedy. The murderer has a ferocious appearance, but is quite mentally ill. He侃侃侃protected the situation of killing his brother without any concealment, and said that he wanted to harm me, so I struck first.

The Nantong County Government found that there were many reactionary slogans in the city and ordered areas. (2) The school authorities should implement strict inspections, pay attention to students' actions, and strictly stipulate leave regulations. (3) The Public Security Bureau should arrest students with improper behavior at any time and notify the school where the student is studying to send someone to the bureau to identify them. (4) The Administrative Commissioners' Office should assign police groups to patrol from time to time.

Fortunately, the water situation has gradually subsided recently, otherwise the consequences would have been disastrous. Gaoyou Eighty-Year-Old Man Drowns Himself

Hu Zicai, an elderly man in Hujia Village, 4th District of the county, who is nearly eighty years old, has always had the worries of Bo Tao. His wife also passed away early. In the past, he made a living by teaching. Now, due to his advanced age, he relies on his nephew for a living. For some reason, Hu suddenly had the idea of ​​ending his life in recent months. He suddenly hanged himself twice last month, but was fortunately rescued both times. However, the night before, Hu took advantage of the people's sleep and went to the river in the 里许 neighborhood to commit suicide. When he was discovered the next morning, he was already dead. It was also tragic.

The criminal knew that he had committed many crimes and had no hope of living, so on the night of the 27th, he took advantage of the guards' sleep, broke through the wall and escaped. Because he was wearing shackles, he could not escape far, so he went to the Huxi Octagon Building and drowned himself.

Naming Ceremony for the Shanghai City Aircraft Held Yesterday 78

Mayor Wu's Wife Performs the Bottle-Breaking Ceremony and Ascends Skyward

The Ministry of Military Affairs Dispatches Ge Jing'en as Representative to Receive

Over Fifty Thousand People Attend the Viewing at Jiangwan

The Shanghai Chinese Aviation Association raised donations for national salvation through aviation and purchased eighteen Hawk fighter planes from the Curtiss Aeroplane and Motor Company in the United States. One has already been shipped, and the remaining seventeen will arrive in Shanghai successively before mid-August. Yesterday at 10:00 AM, the renowned American pilot Major Doolittle flew the aircraft around the city for a week, distributing leaflets and slogans to promote the public's ambition to save the nation through aviation. At 2:00 PM in the afternoon, the naming ceremony for the Shanghai City aircraft was held at the Jiangwan Racecourse. Major Doolittle also piloted the aircraft to perform various stunts. Simultaneously, American aviator Lewis Duxton Kong Wu performed a mid-air jump. Over fifty thousand citizens went to the Jiangwan Racecourse yesterday to watch,

making it a grand occasion. The details are recorded below:

City Flyover

The Shanghai Chinese Aviation Association, in order to promote public awareness of aviation and national salvation through aviation, had American pilot Major Doolittle fly the aircraft from Longhua at 10:00 AM yesterday, circling the city for a week. He also scattered a large number of leaflets from the air. The content of the leaflets was divided into five types, all encouraging citizens to participate in national salvation through aviation. At 11:00 AM, he flew to the Jiangwan Racecourse and landed.

Ge Arrives in Shanghai

Aviation Director Ge Jing'en, upon the orders of the government and the Ministry of Military Affairs, came to Shanghai to attend the naming ceremony and represent the government in accepting the donated aircraft. At 9:40 AM yesterday, he and the head of the Aviation Department, Shen Dexie, flew from Hangzhou to Shanghai. Mao Bangchu, the principal of the Central Aviation School, was unable to arrive in time as he had flown from Hangzhou to Beijing the day before. Director Ge, Mayor Wu, Lin Wojiang, and others immediately went to the Jiangwan Racecourse. The staff of the Aviation Association and the Solicitation Headquarters had already made arrangements at the site.

Right: Mr. Doolittle (Photo by Dagong She) 79

Venue Arrangement

The Aviation Association dispatched personnel to the racecourse in advance to arrange everything. A stage was set up on the race track opposite the grandstand. The flags of the Party and the nation were hung around the stage. The venue was equipped with wireless broadcasting equipment to amplify the sound so that the entire audience could hear the speeches from the stage. The security of the venue was the responsibility of the Municipal Security Team, the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and the Municipal Defense Regiment. The China Star Film Company and the American Fox Film Company also arrived to film a sound movie to commemorate the event.

Attendees

Yesterday, starting at 1:00 PM, dignitaries and famous people from the city arrived one after another. Those present included Central Representative and Central Bank President Kong Xiangxi and his wife, Minister of the Military Affairs Department Ge Jing'en, Mayor Wu Tiecheng and his wife, Security Director Yang Hu and his wife, Wang Zhengting and his wife, Dai Ji's representative and Chief of Staff of the Garrison Command Zhang Xiang, Jianghai Customs Superintendent Tang Haian, Finance Ministry Secretary Guo Dehua, Public Security Bureau Chief Wen Hongen, Public Works Bureau Chief Xu Peihuang, Health Bureau Chief Li Tingan, Shen Dexie, leaders from all walks of life such as Yu Qiaqing, Shi Liangcai, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Xu Shiying, and others, as well as people from all walks of life and students from various schools, totaling over fifty thousand people.

Order of the Assembly

(1) Music, (2) Singing of the Party Anthem, (3) Paying the Highest Respects to the Party and National Flags and the Portrait of the Premier, (4) Chairman Reverently Reads the Premier's Will, (5) Report, (6) Speech, (7) Naming Ceremony, (8) Aircraft Handover Ceremony, (9) Sky Ascension Ceremony, (10) Performance, (11) Music, (12) Ceremony Concluded. The presidium of the assembly was composed of Wu Tiecheng, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Shi Liangcai, and Lin Kanghou. Kong Xiangxi and Ge Jing'en were specially dispatched by the central government to participate in the ceremony. Mayor Wu performed the naming ceremony, presidium member Yu Qiaqing and Aviation Director Ge Jing'en performed the aircraft handover ceremony, and Mayor Wu's wife performed the sky ascension ceremony.

Chairman's Report

The naming ceremony began at 2:30 PM in the afternoon. After the ceremony was performed in accordance with the rituals, Wang Xiaolai of the presidium gave a report, stating briefly that the Chinese Aviation Association's solicitation team had ordered eighteen fighter planes in the first batch. Today was the day to hold the naming ceremony for the first Shanghai City aircraft. This aircraft can be said to be an aircraft of patriotism and resistance against Japan through the united cooperation of the people and the government. Today we arrived at Jiangwan, and along the way we witnessed the tragic situation. In addition, we don't know what the situation in North China and the current state of Tianjin and Beijing are. We can only endure hardship and strive to strengthen ourselves through aviation to save the nation, completely to consolidate national defense and strengthen our strength. We must also pay attention to three points simultaneously: (1) Aviation to save the nation, (2) Abolish civil war, (3) Promote domestic goods. These three points cannot be achieved solely by relying on the government; the people must work together, and so on.

Kong's Speech

Next, Kong Xiangxi, the special representative of the central government, gave a speech, stating briefly that today is the day for all compatriots to donate the first aircraft to the national government for naming. He was deeply impressed and admired. The Premier advocated saving the nation through aviation, and we should strive to follow his lead in developing the country. In recent centuries, military warfare has evolved from planar to three-dimensional, relying entirely on the strength of the air force. As Marshal Foch said, "An air force

Center: Director Ge Jing'en (Photo by Li Zunyong) 80

is the main force for victory or defeat in war." The January 28th Incident and the anti-Japanese military affairs in North China both failed due to the lack of an air force. Therefore, to consolidate national defense, we must develop aviation. Especially, the government and the people must cooperate fully. The Shanghai citizens, under the leadership of Mayor Wu, have shown the initial expression of cooperation with the Shanghai aircraft. He hoped that the public would enthusiastically donate so that the fleet could be expanded from the first team to ten teams and dozens of teams to contribute to the national aviation construction and achieve it as soon as possible. With these eighteen aircraft, the government can form a squadron. He hopes that the citizens of all provinces will rise up and donate a squadron of aircraft each to promote aviation construction, so that we can resist the enemy in the shortest possible time. However, this responsibility relies entirely on the power of the masses and should be demonstrated through practical actions rather than just words.

Mayor's Speech

Next, Mayor Wu gave a speech, stating briefly that today the Chinese Aviation Association is holding the naming ceremony for the first Shanghai City aircraft. Tiecheng is honored to attend this grand ceremony, and in addition to his joy, he dares to express his most sincere feelings and his deep expectations. A country must have a foundation to stand on. If a country does not have a strong foundation, the nation will lose its guarantee of life. In ancient times, the major affairs of the country were sacrifice and war. Confucius also emphasized "sufficient troops" when discussing politics. Examining the path of development of various countries in modern times and quietly studying the examples of national revival, all are the same. Unfortunately, our people are ignorant of the bond of "peace" and "struggle" and neglect the cultivation of national military power. Living in danger and seeking ease, they do not know how to be invigorated. National defense is lax, and all barriers have been removed. Foreign forces invade and cannot be stopped. Descending to the present day, we are deeply mired in an unprecedented predicament. The Chinese Aviation Association, based on the principle of saving the nation through aviation, supports the government and builds the air force. For several months, they have been running around and appealing, sincerely asking for contributions from all walks of life and generous donations. They have raised huge amounts of funds for national salvation through aviation. Now, the Chinese Aviation Association has ordered eighteen fighter planes from the Curtiss Company in the United States, and the first Shanghai City aircraft will hold a grand and solemn naming ceremony today. This is something we cannot help but feel gratified about. Today, this first Shanghai City aircraft will gallop in the clear sky and initially test its heroism and develop its power. We must know that this first Shanghai City aircraft soaring in the clear sky is the pioneer of our national revolution, the savior of our national life, the new engine of our national self-improvement, and the symbol of our national rejuvenation. All Chinese people must not ignore it. Now, at the time of naming, consider its name [Center: Mrs. Wu (Photo by Li Zunyong) P>

and think of its meaning, mourn the national crisis, and thoroughly recognize the profound and great significance of today's naming ceremony, and think about striving forward. However, since the European War, the air force has been the center of modern national defense plans. World powers are concentrating their financial resources and national power to engage in the construction of the air force. Statistics on the existing air force strength of various countries and the number of aircraft range from more than ten thousand to several thousand. Comparing each other, the strength and weakness are immediately apparent. How can we be complacent with just a few aircraft and should deeply alert ourselves, catch up quickly, and continue our efforts to complete the great cause of saving the nation? As the saying goes, "It is simple to start, but it will be huge to finish." Although we cannot be complacent, we don't need to be discouraged. The survival of the nation and the rise and fall of the country depend on the efforts of the people from now on.

Mayor Unveils the Flag

The Shanghai City aircraft is painted brown, and the wings are yellow. The words "Curtiss Eagle" are written in the middle of the fuselage. The head and both wings are covered with the flags of the Party and the nation. After Mayor Wu finished his speech, he and his wife went down from the stage and stood on the left and right sides in front of the aircraft. Miss Gan Shuxian and Zhang Guiqing also stood in front of the left and right wings. Mayor Wu then made a simple speech and unveiled the flag of the Party and the nation covering the head of the aircraft. At the same time, Miss Gan and Zhang also unveiled the flags of the Party and the nation on the left and right wings, and the naming ceremony ended.

Aircraft Handover Ceremony

After the naming, Chairman Yu Qiaqing presented the aircraft certificate to Director Ge. The upper end of the aircraft certificate was the Premier's will. The middle text stated, "I have found that the state has the right to defend, and individuals have the duty to donate. Now, I respectfully present the Shanghai City fighter plane purchased by this association to the government to defend against insults and protect the people. Each shall fulfill his or her responsibilities, which is the boundless blessing of the Party and the nation. This is the certificate." Below were the signatures of the Chinese Aviation Association and the date. After Ge received the certificate, he gave a speech saying that today, Jing'en represents the government in accepting the fighter plane donated by the Chinese Aviation Association. The enthusiasm of the Shanghai compatriots and all comrades of the Aviation Association for national defense is greatly admired. This aircraft will be designated as the first aircraft of the Air Force Fighter Squadron. He hopes that the public will help the government, and that with the leadership and promotion of all the compatriots in Shanghai and all the colleagues of the Aviation Association, we will go from one aircraft to one squadron, and from one squadron to dozens of squadrons. Jing'en and the Chinese Air Force will surely repay the compatriots of the whole country, make the air defense solid, and the country will no longer suffer losses, and bring our country to a rich and strong region, starting today.

Performing Stunts

After the aircraft handover ceremony, Mayor Wu's wife performed the bottle-breaking ceremony. She gently threw a bottle of champagne at the engine of the aircraft. The champagne splashed everywhere, and the crowd cheered. At 3:15 PM, Major Doolittle finished boarding the aircraft and took off after starting the engine. (1) First, he flew high to ten thousand feet, then gradually descended, performing a straight drop and straight ascent. (2) He performed various spins and inversions at high altitude. (3) He descended again to perform side flight, inverted flight, slow flight, and fast flight. (4) He performed a falling-leaf-style fluttering ascent and descent, without any sound. (5) He performed a sharp-angle turning flight. (6) He performed a body-downward-falling-style flight. The performance lasted about twenty minutes before he gracefully descended. His flying skills had indeed reached the peak, and his amazing stunts were praised by the crowd. At the thrilling parts of the performance, everyone was speechless. When he turned danger into safety and ascended straight into the sky, they stomped their feet and exclaimed.

Mid-Air Jumping Performance

After Doolittle's performance, Curtiss Company prepared another training aircraft, with yellow wings as well, but it could carry two people in the front and rear. American aviator Lewis drove it, and Duxton performed a safe parachute jump. The training aircraft first flew low around the field for a week, scattering flowers in the air to celebrate the success of saving the nation through aviation. Finally, he flew high to more than five thousand feet, and Duxton, with a safety parachute strapped to his back, jumped from the high altitude. The safety parachute immediately opened and floated down, with a beautiful posture. The applause was thunderous. Before long, he safely landed on the racecourse. At exactly 4:00 PM, the various performances ended, and the meeting was adjourned with music.

Flying Back to Longhua

After the aerial performance and the adjournment with music, Major Doolittle still flew the Shanghai City aircraft back to Longhua Airport for parking. According to Ge Jing'en, the director of the Aviation Department who was specially assigned by the central government to receive the aircraft, after the Shanghai City aircraft is received, it will be temporarily parked at Longhua Airport for two or three days. Then, Shen Dexie, the director of the aircraft factory, will fly it to Hangzhou, and after all the repainting is completed, it will be flown to Nanjing and incorporated into the Air Force. He himself will stay in Shanghai for a short time, or return to Hangzhou on the same plane.

Mayor's Remarks

While Major Doolittle was performing stunts in the air, reporters approached Mayor Wu to ask about the price of the order. He replied that the Aviation Association ordered eighteen Hawk fighter planes from the Curtiss Company in the United States, costing approximately US$400,000 and some odd numbers. Currently, the value of the US dollar is slightly lower, so it is roughly equivalent to 1.7 million to 1.8 million Chinese currency. The average price per aircraft is around 100,000 yuan. The remaining seventeen aircraft will be shipped to Shanghai successively before mid-August. Also, when Mr. Duxton performed the safe parachute descent, his posture was very beautiful, and Mayor Wu also clapped his hands and praised it. He told reporters that the safe parachute performance is very risky and cannot be done without rich experience. The price of each safety parachute is approximately US$2,000.

One Aircraft Damaged

After the Curtiss Company's training aircraft completed the first act of its performance on the field, it descended from the western end of the racecourse at 3:50 PM. When it was about to touch the ground, only three or four feet away, it suddenly and inadvertently caused the wheels to touch the low railing of the race track. As a result, the aircraft moved forward and was obstructed. The right wheel immediately broke, and the aircraft fell to the ground. At that moment, the audience was shocked and clamored, rushing forward to see. Member of the Central Committee Kong Xiangxi and Mayor Wu Tiecheng and others, upon hearing the sound, immediately went to investigate. At this time, the pilot, Mr. Lewis, had already smiled and jumped out of the aircraft. Wu and Kong immediately stepped forward to shake hands and express their concern, asking if he was injured. Mr. Lewis smiled and said no. They then inspected the aircraft, and except for the right wheel falling into the small river beside the field, there was no other damage. Thereupon, the crowd was slightly relieved.

One Person Crushed to Death

After the aircraft left, the audience dispersed, and Jiangwan Road became even more crowded. At 4:50 PM, at the corner of Jiangwan Road and Tiyu Association Road, a local accent aged over ten years was injured by a public bus in the crowd and died immediately.

Huang Shaoxiong Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 81

Talks about the Situation in North China

and the Ceasefire Negotiations

Central News Agency reported that Minister of the Interior Huang Shaoxiong arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning and returned to his new residence on West Aixin Road to rest. A Central News Agency reporter went to ask him about the recent situation in North China and the process of signing the Sino-Japanese ceasefire agreement. He answered in detail. The details are recorded as follows:

The Central Government Will Issue a Declaration

Mr. Huang said that he had reported on the recent situation in North China at the Lushan Conference on his trip south to Xun, but he did not participate in the meeting, so he did not know the details of the meeting. However, according to what he knew, after the signing of the Sino-Japanese ceasefire agreement, the central government will issue a declaration within days, reporting in detail the process of signing the Sino-Japanese ceasefire, so that the whole country can fully understand.

The Agreement Did Not Involve Politics

The ceasefire agreement has been formally signed. According to what he knew about the negotiations, the representatives of both sides were all military personnel, and no political representatives attended. The scope of the discussion was limited to military affairs and did not involve politics. Huang Yongbai, the chairman of the Political Affairs Sorting Committee stationed in Peiping, was only in an assisting position in the ceasefire negotiations and did not participate in the negotiations. The rumors were all speculation. The first article of the agreement stipulates that the Chinese army shall withdraw from Yanqing, Changping, Gaoliying, Shunyi, Tongzhou, Xianghe, Baodi, Linyin, Ninghe, Lutai, and the area west and south of the line connected by them and shall not advance. In fact, most of the above-mentioned locations have been occupied by the Japanese army. As for the security of the area about a hundred miles south of the Great Wall, it is maintained by the local authorities with police force.

The Northeast Issue Was Not Discussed

The ceasefire negotiations have now come to an end. The rumors that the ceasefire negotiations were carried out in two steps, the first step being military in nature and the second step being political in nature, were unknown to him. The Northeast issue was not discussed in this ceasefire negotiation. In the future, China and Japan may conduct separate negotiations to resolve the outstanding issues between China and Japan, but he dare not predict this. However, the ceasefire negotiations in North China have now come to an end, and there is no so-called "second step" of negotiation.

Three Hopes for the Future

Mr. Huang also said that because our army's combat equipment is far inferior to that of the enemy, although we resisted to the death, we did not achieve the goal of recovering lost territory. As a last resort, we negotiated a ceasefire. Now the war has temporarily come to an end. We can only hope for (1) rectifying military affairs, because our military aircraft are all old-fashioned, and even fighting with broadswords against artillery fire, the outcome of the battle can be known without fighting. Therefore, without immediate rectification, it is not enough to resist strong enemies. (2) Solidarity between the upper and lower levels. Now our people's hearts are scattered, which is enough to invite foreign insults. If we are determined to resist the enemy, we cannot do it without solidarity between the upper and lower levels. (3) Recognizing the country. The people should understand the government's measures and intentions, and unity between the upper and lower levels can be realized. The above three items, he hopes that the government and the people will pay attention to them together.

Anti-Japanese War Does Not Advocate Empty Talk

Member of the Central Committee Feng Yuxiang recently telegraphed to take office as the commander-in-chief of the Anti-Japanese Allied Army. Huang said that he did not know what the central government's attitude was, and he did not know whether it had been discussed at the Lushan Conference. In short, the anti-Japanese work is in practice, not in chanting slogans. Furthermore, if Feng is determined to resist Japan, why not implement it earlier, and wait until the anti-Japanese armies are all exhausted and unable to fight before mobilizing, it seems too late. The situation in Chahar is currently extremely chaotic. Chairman Song of Chahar Province is now busy rescuing the wounded and caring for the dead. It is incomprehensible that Feng has arbitrarily changed the chairman of Chahar Province. Mr. Huang did not want to express his opinion on the Southwest issue. He has not decided when to go north again. However, he knew that Mr. Huang would stay in Shanghai for about two or three days.

Ma Xiangbo and Zhang Taiyan Telegraphically Encourage Feng Yuxiang 82

Following the People of the Whole Country

As a Backing for Your Service

Ninety-four-year-old Ma Xiangbo and national scholar Zhang Taiyan sympathized with Feng Yuxiang's anti-Japanese proposition in the telegram, and sent a telegram to Zhangjiakou to express their condolences and encouragement. The original text is recorded below: To Commander-in-Chief Feng Huanzhang of the Anti-Japanese Allied Army of the People of Zhangjiakou, I have received your telegram. Japan is showing its insatiable desire, and the ashes of Manchuria are burning again. The authorities regard it as a minor skin disease that cannot be cured. The internal organs are all decayed. He will not discuss the others. Even in the city of Beiping, the Japanese soldiers who have entered are two thousand five hundred, even searching houses and patrolling the East City. Our military police retreat with caution. Is it still said that Beiping has not been lost? If the compromise is quickly reached and the Japanese soldiers temporarily retreat, but the heavy door is wide open, and there is no restriction on coming and going, in just a few years, the area north of the Yellow River will be occupied by the enemy. The people can't bear it and appeal to you. You respond to the urgent demands with a firm character. Although the start is late, it meets the times. Although the place is small, it is connected to the hearts of the people. The one who mourns wins in battle. You and the people of Chahar Province can be said to be the ones who mourn. If the defense of Chahar is solid, it must ensure that the facilities in North China are complete before we can rely on it without fear. Then, if the east has not been determined in Shenyang and the north has not been recovered in Rehe, there is no time when we are not in mourning. Japan has been a disaster in the east for forty years. The invasion of Manchuria has had Chinese soil for more than two hundred and ninety years. Fortunately, during the Xinhai Revolution, the people cooperated to restore the old things. Although the harm of Manchuria has been removed, the disaster of Japan has not been eliminated. Now, due to the authorities' negligence, the two thieves are working together, endangering the Olympic area. If this is not treated, it is not only ignoring foreign troubles, but also completely abandoning the merits of the Xinhai Revolution. You have been involved in the uprising in Luozhou for more than thirty years and have not forgotten the old things. You have gathered righteous people and used white cloth as funds. The place you occupy, Chahar, was originally the old commandery of Yunzhong Dingxiang in the Qin and Han dynasties of the Seven Kingdoms. How is it different from Guo Fenyang's uprising in Shuofang? Your heart is enough to represent the hearts of those who have blood in the whole country. Your words are enough to represent the words of those who have blood in the whole country. Your actions will be able to thoroughly lead the actions of those who have blood in the whole country. Although some are in their twilight years, if there is still a breath left, they will follow the people of the whole country as a backing for your service. Only uphold righteousness and move forward, and do not look around at all. Ma Liang, Zhang Binglin,

The Civil Service Disciplinary Committee Was Officially Established Yesterday 85

The Shanghai Municipal Local Civil Service Disciplinary Committee was officially established yesterday. At the same time, the first meeting was held, and the rules of procedure for the clerks were approved. The details are recorded below:

Attending Members The association was officially established at 10:00 a.m. yesterday, and the ceremony was held in the meeting room of the local court. Due to the national crisis, everything was simplified. In addition to Chairman Shen Xiqing, members Zhao Shulan, Yao Fuxiang, Qian Chengjun, Pang Rong, Luo Ren, Li Suixian, Sun Pu, Pan Ge, Zhu Fengwei and others were present. They arrived at the meeting one after another before 9 o'clock and attended in person.

Meeting Situation The founding conference was held at 10:00 a.m. and the first meeting continued. After the ceremony, Chairman Shen Xiqing presided over the meeting. Shen reported (1) the establishment of the association, (2) the number of members and seats of the association, and (3) the number of clerks of the association and the situation of transferring concurrent positions. After the chairman's report, two motions were discussed and resolved. (1) To set the number and date of regular meetings, it was passed that they would be held at 10:00 a.m. on the second Wednesday of each month. (2) The rules of procedure for the clerks of the association were adopted. The meeting was adjourned at 11:00 a.m. for photography and refreshments.

Assigned Staff The staff of the association were all transferred from the personnel of the local court, and they held concurrent positions without additional pay to save money. They were also announced at the same time yesterday. Chairman Shen appointed Wang Daozhou, the court clerk, as the director of affairs, and Yin Wenlian, Xiong Nianpeng, Zhou Mingxian, and Fan Shengyang as the clerks (all of whom were court clerks).

Establishment Announcement After the establishment of the association, in addition to reporting to the Administrative Court, the first announcement was issued, saying, "For the purpose of announcement, the National Government's Judicial Yuan, Order No. 84, dispatched Shen Xiqing to concurrently serve as the chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Local Civil Service Disciplinary Committee, and the National Government's Judicial Yuan, Instruction No. 127, issued a copper seal with the words "Shanghai Municipal Local Civil Service Disciplinary Committee Seal", and a small copper seal with the words "Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Local Civil Service Disciplinary Committee", and ordered the dispatch of various concurrent committee members, and ordered that the establishment of the organization and the date of the use of the seal be reported for record. For the above reasons, the chairman immediately convened all the committee members to form an organization and use the seal on June 1 of this year. In addition to reporting the order separately, it is appropriate to issue an announcement for public knowledge. This is hereby announced. Chairman Shen Xiqing."

The Bureau of Navigation Affairs Convened a Conference of Directors from Various Locations Yesterday 90

Revising the Method of Issuing Ship Route Certificates, etc.

The Shanghai Bureau of Navigation Affairs of the Ministry of Communications, in order to manage ships and issue ship route certificates, convened a conference of directors of offices from various locations at its office at 10:00 AM yesterday. Yu Sen from Wuhu, Yu Shiying from Zhenjiang, Yu Jiufeng from Wenzhou, Tu Zongsheng from Ningbo, Wang Maoqin from Haizhou, and the director of the bureau, Zhu Yaoting, secretary Chen Yongjie, section chiefs Chen Yici, and Yu Shifan were present. Director Zhu presided over the meeting and the following proposals were discussed: (1) Proposed amendments to the interim measures for issuing ship route certificates: The chairman submitted the proposal for discussion, and it was passed with amendments. (2) It was suggested that each office should investigate the living conditions of ships and sailors in its jurisdiction in order to design improvements. The Haizhou office proposed, and the principle was approved. The bureau will compile a form and hand it over to each office to begin the investigation. (3) It was suggested that increasing the trust of sailors should start from striving for their convenience. The Haizhou office proposed, and the principle was approved. (4) It was suggested to reissue sailboat licenses for free to unify them and facilitate examination. The Haizhou office proposed, and it was shelved. (5) It was suggested to reissue tonnage certificates for free in cases of measurement or calculation errors by previous measurers to show solemnity. The Haizhou office proposed, and it was noted that the bureau had already issued an order to all offices to comply with this, so there was no need for further discussion. (6) It was suggested to submit a "Four-Column Table of Book and Card Data" on a monthly basis. The Haizhou office proposed, and it was passed. (7) The opinion on the 1933 budget of the Haizhou office was submitted for discussion. The Haizhou office proposed. (8) The proposal to draft and extract the 1933 budget of the Wuhu office was submitted for discussion. The Wuhu office proposed. The first and second cases were handed over to the First Section for reference when preparing the 1933 budget for each office. (9) The establishment of auxiliary agencies was proposed by the Wenzhou office, and it was decided that there was no need to establish separate agencies. (10) A draft of the uniform hat for staff was proposed by the Wenzhou office, and it was passed. The bureau will draft a style. (11) It was proposed that the ship clearance procedures should first be reported to the customs office with a voucher issued by the Bureau of Navigation Affairs or its office. The Zhenjiang office proposed, and it was postponed. (12) The Zhenjiang office proposed that the competition in the shipping industry, which is related to navigation safety, should be prohibited to avoid danger and that separate measures should be formulated. (13) The Wuhu office proposed to reorganize the shipping industry. The opening of a shipping company should be submitted by the Bureau of Navigation Affairs to the Ministry of Communications for approval. (14) The Zhenjiang office proposed to add navigation police to protect them, which should be planned by the bureau as a whole. (15) The Zhenjiang office proposed that the organization of shipping guilds or similar institutions in various places, as well as gatherings related to navigation administration, should be submitted to the competent authorities for record or sent to the case for filing and reported to the Ministry for forwarding to the Central Party Headquarters to instruct the relevant local party headquarters to inform them. (16) The Zhenjiang office proposed that the passenger fares of each ship should be submitted to the Bureau of Navigation Affairs for approval and should not be increased or decreased without authorization to eliminate malpractices and demonstrate uniformity, which should be planned by the bureau as a whole. The meeting adjourned at 5:30 PM.

The Datong Music Society Adds Students to Its National Music Specialization Program 95

The Datong Music Society of Shanghai, after its first joint performance with Western music at the Grand Theater the day before yesterday, although not a failure, had fewer members in its orchestra than the Western orchestra. Moreover, the society has more than 180 kinds of musical instruments and of course wants to make them all sound, so as not to lose the original intention of manufacturing them. In the future, there will be a second joint performance of Chinese and Western orchestras. Based on these two reasons, it is really necessary to expand the orchestra. Cultivating talents is especially urgent. The Society plans to upgrade the qualifications of its existing members (awarding prizes, giving certificates, and recommending them to serve as national music educators in schools) and re-establish new regulations. In the future, new members joining the Datong Orchestra must first serve as students for five months of study and pass the grades of various musical instruments stipulated by the society before they can join. It has now started recruiting 100 students and is scheduled to start registration on June 1st and officially start classes on the 11th. The musical notation used is edited with a comparison of staff notation and gongche notation for each instrument, with basic exercises for each. The guqin and pipa are used as regular courses, and the monthly fee is 5 yuan (including lecture notes and instrument fees). The regulations can be obtained from the Society. Those who aspire to national music should not miss this opportunity.
