Record of the Annual Meeting of the Taishan Insurance Company 97

Xu Xinliu Gives a Speech

The Taishan Insurance Company at No. 2 Beijing Road is the only sound insurance company organized with Chinese capital. It has been operating various types of water, fire, life, and accident insurance businesses since it opened in the autumn of last year. The company convened its first annual shareholders' meeting the day before yesterday on the second floor of the company. All shareholders attended. In addition to reporting various accounts, business conditions, and passing various motions (omitted), Mr. Xu Xinliu, chairman of the company, gave a detailed report. The recording of his speech is as follows: "Distinguished shareholders, today is the first annual shareholders' meeting of our company. I am very happy to be able to gather with all of you and report on the company's financial results and all other circumstances. Our company has only been in existence for five months since the capital was fully paid up on August 1 last year and the company was established. The actual start of business was on September 21, and it has only been a little more than three months until the end of the year. The time is very short, so the accounts presented to you today only represent the activities of more than three months and have not been able to fully express the company's operating conditions. Although the company's business hours were only more than three months, the progress was quite smooth. Within three months, the total premium income reached 75,014 yuan, 9 jiao, and 8 fen. For a company that has just been founded, it seems to be a considerable number in a very short period of time, and it is reassuring to all shareholders. Now, I would like to report the company's business policy and the calculation of donations, the balance sheet of assets and liabilities, etc. as follows: The company's original business has four types: water insurance, fire insurance, accident insurance, and life insurance. The Board of Directors and the executives agree that the business policy should be to develop all four businesses equally, and it is not appropriate to focus on one type. Therefore, all premium income should be weighed according to the circumstances and balanced, and not concentrated on any one party. Please divide the situation of the four businesses and report them separately. Fire insurance is an important part of the insurance business, and our company will naturally operate it with the utmost care. However, in the past, Chinese insurance companies have tended to focus on this one way, resulting in fierce competition and repeated reductions in premium prices. At the same time, the solicitation of orders must also be done with the utmost caution. Now, our company's business policy, although paying great attention to fire insurance, is not biased towards it, in order to achieve parallel progress. The water insurance item is currently only doing foreign business. The executive department believes that Chinese companies have a lot of room for development in this business. The accident insurance part can get income immediately, and it is a stable and good business in the insurance industry. However, it is still in the experimental stage, and the risk of operating it alone is relatively large. It is better to contact the same industry and work together, then the strength will be great, the effect will be fast, and the risk will be less. Therefore, our company is now jointly operated by several insurance companies in this port, in order to be stable and reliable. Life insurance can not only seek security for the insured and their families, but also absorb scattered funds to create huge funds for the revitalization of various industries. It can be said that the method is good and the meaning is beautiful. However, this kind of insurance in our country is not very developed. Among the 400 million people, the number of insured is still less than 30,000. If we can solicit it properly, the future hope is very high. Therefore, our company pays very close attention to this kind of insurance. In the three-month period of this financial settlement, we have received an insured amount of 514,000 yuan, and the solicitation cost is only 8,698 yuan, 8 jiao, and 3 fen, which seems to be worthwhile. The reserves for the above-mentioned fire insurance, water insurance, and accident insurance departments have been clarified and burdened in accordance with the contract, and the outstanding capital has been withdrawn as of December 31, and the accounting is accurate, which is sufficient to cope with all claims responsibilities. There is profit and no deficit, and its life insurance reserves are handled in accordance with the American death table. The first year's premium is used as a calculation system for term insurance, and is provided in full, and a weekly interest rate of 3.5% is guaranteed, which can be said to have a completely reliable guarantee for the interests of the insured. As for the profit and loss statement, this term originally had no losses and should be listed as surplus, but there are no loss and surplus items in the book, because our company should first consolidate its foundation when it was first founded. Therefore, all the benefits were allocated to the start-up costs, providing sufficient reserves, and eliminating the cost of generating wealth, decoration, and annual depreciation of 50%, etc. In this way, the foundation is solid, and it will be easier to succeed in future development. This method must be approved by all shareholders. Also, in this term, the cash item in the liability schedule is quite large, because the time is very short during this period, and the situation is not very stable, so we did not dare to invest rashly, so there is this temporary phenomenon. However, the amount invested in this term has also increased slightly, totaling 3,017 yuan, 3 jiao, and 8 fen. This increase has been transferred to the investment change reserve. The company's investment list and report card are all recorded, and you can read them to understand them. Also, during this period, although there were very few compensation events, the agents' commissions were paid in advance, and at the same time, premium reserves had to be provided. At the time of closing, the policies were not yet mature, and the premiums that had not yet expired were not listed in the accounts. Therefore, the income and expenditure seem to be not very balanced. This is the phenomenon that should exist in the trend of events. Added attachments, in addition, there are incidental reports, which are that all the service personnel of the company, all the staff of the executive department, are familiar with their efforts and loyal to their duties, which is deeply gratifying and grateful to the company, and can be reported to all shareholders. However, the wisdom of neighbors and others is short-sighted, and I hope that all shareholders will not hesitate to give guidance at any time.

Nuo Na and Zhang Jia Living Buddhas Elected as Supervisors

Wang Yiting, Guan Jiongzhi, and Others Elected as Executive Committee Members

The Chinese Buddhist Association held its fifth National Buddhist Representatives Assembly at the Jueyuan on Hart Road at 10:00 AM yesterday. Details are recorded below:

Delegates Present

Attendees included ex officio delegates Nuo Na Living Buddha, Zhang Jia Living Buddha, Wang Yiting, Kai Jiongzhi, Huang Hanzhi, Wen Lanting, Zhong Kanghou, and others; as well as Jiangsu delegate Juehui, Zhejiang delegate Baojing, Shaanxi delegate Kang Jiyao, Fujian delegate Ri, Anhui delegate Huang Jianliu, Hubei delegate Chi Huan, Yunnan delegate Dayuan, Henan delegate Xi Jing, Hunan delegate Lisheng, Nanjing City delegate Yu Shan, Shanghai City delegate Yuanchen, and sixty-five others. They do not know that our Buddha, with a great fearless spirit, embraces the enthusiasm to save the world and all living beings, without competing for gain and loss, and with equality between enemies and relatives. This has been clearly instructed in the teachings. I hope that in the future, we will pay attention to the following points: (1) self-awareness and awakening others, (2) saving the country and the world, (3) actively promoting social work, so that Buddhism can flourish and become the only treasure to save the world, remedy society, and universally liberate all living beings." After Sino-Russian Trade, National Vessels Navigate to Vladivostok 100

Zhongwei Shunfeng Wheel

First Ship to Russia

Trial Voyage

Since the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, more and more Soviet goods have been imported into China. The Soviet merchant fleet has sent six ships to and from Shanghai and Vladivostok. Recently, a large number of Russian goods such as wood, Kimura glass, and flower-labeled kerosene have been shipped to Shanghai. Besides Russian ships, no other country's merchant ships operate on this route. Mr. Chen Shuntong, the owner of the Huashang Zhongwei Wheel Company, recently decided to operate the company's new Shunfeng ship, which has a load capacity of 8,000 tons and is most suitable for sailing on the outer sea route, on the Sino-Russian route, taking advantage of the beginning of Sino-Russian trade. The first trial voyage to Vladivostok, loading cargo to and from, is scheduled to depart from Shanghai today. The route will take it to Lushun, Dalian, Japan, and then to Vladivostok.

Loading Wood

The Shunfeng ship is very large. This time, it is sailing to Vladivostok to transport 1.8 million cubic feet of Russian wood purchased by Shanghai Chinese merchants to Shanghai, as well as other Russian goods. It is scheduled to depart from Shanghai to Vladivostok today. Because the shipping schedule is tight, no goods are being shipped from Shanghai. Many goods bound for Russia will be unloaded in Lushun. Mr. Chen has telegraphed the manager in Lushun to prepare.

Prohibitions

The Shunfeng ship is the first national vessel to sail on the Sino-Russian route after the resumption of diplomatic relations between the two countries. Vladivostok's inspection of foreign ships entering the port is very strict. Crew members are not allowed to bring any items ashore. Even spare items on board must be reported in advance. Any omissions will be fined. After arriving in Vladivostok, only Russian currency can be used, but it is forbidden to privately export Russian gold coins. Violators will be severely punished. Yesterday, Mr. Chen Shuntong thoroughly informed the crew of these details of entering Vladivostok and instructed them to comply.

Tong Baoren Assassinated 101

Sudden Attack by Seven Thugs

Wife Screams for Help After Husband Dies

Tong Baoren, a native of Shaoxing, 44 years old, has been running the Yongli Dyeing Workshop at No. 97, Lane 2, Puyu East Road, outside Dananmen, Nanshi, for more than ten years. Because Tong is honest and hardworking, his business has been quite successful. Yesterday morning around 5:00 AM, when the workers in the workshop had already gotten up and were working in the workshop, seven thugs suddenly arrived. Two of them guarded the gate, and the rest broke into the workshop. The leader, wearing a gray cloth gown, about twenty years old, speaking with a Shaoxing accent, seemed afraid of being recognized, so he wore a pair of black glasses on his nose. He pointed a pistol and drove the workers to a corner, forbidding them from making any noise, and left two people to monitor them. They went straight into Tong's bedroom. At that time, Tong happened to be sleeping in the same bed with his wife, Ms. Xie, and had not yet gotten up. However, the thugs were very familiar with the situation in the workshop. After breaking into Tong's bedroom, they went straight to Tong's bedside. When they lifted the bed curtain, Tong had already woken up. He immediately sat up and asked, "What are you doing here?" He tried to get up and grab the thug, but the thug immediately pulled the trigger and fired a shot at Tong. There was a crisp sound, and the bullet entered Tong's left breast and exited from his left waist. He was injured instantly, bleeding profusely. He screamed miserably, fell back on the bed, and died. Ms. Xie was sitting next to Tong and was shocked to see this tragic scene. She screamed for help on the bed. The thugs, seeing that their goal had been achieved, strode out and left with their accomplices in the workshop, fleeing towards Dananmen. Afterwards, Ms. Xie immediately reported the situation to the Third Precinct of the First District. After hearing the report, Chief Jin immediately dispatched a large number of police officers to search everywhere, but it had been a long time, and the thugs had already fled far away, so they did not catch them. Later, Police Chief Wang Zuoxian was sent to investigate the workshop. In Tong's bedroom, they found a white Lysol pistol bullet casing. According to Tong's wife, the deceased had no enemies outside, so the reason for the murder was really unclear. She reported the situation to the chief. Because the case was bizarre and involved human life, in addition to ordering the arrest of the murderer, the twenty-third patrolman Qin Defang was dispatched to report to the Shanghai Local Court for an autopsy.

Fifth District of the County Petitions for Establishment of Branch Hospital 102

Xing Zhigang, the magistrate of the fifth district of Shanghai County, yesterday submitted a document to Cao, the Administrative Inspector of the Fifth District of Jiangsu Province and concurrent County Magistrate, petitioning to forward a letter to the Public Shanghai Hospital, requesting the establishment of a branch hospital within the jurisdiction of the district to benefit the poor and sick and to care for the lives of the people. The district established a free medical clinic for the poor last summer, and hundreds of people from far and wide come to seek medical treatment every day. However, it is limited to various departments of traditional Chinese medicine. When there are acute infectious diseases, it is often difficult to treat them, and people are forced to wait for death. It is not as effective as the precise and rapid surgery of Western medicine, which is a pity. Since the beginning of this summer, seasonal diseases have been rampant. Although there is a long-standing wish to continue running the free clinic, it is impossible to raise funds due to the lack of public funds. Recently, I heard that your office sent a letter to the Public Shanghai Hospital, requesting the establishment of a branch hospital in the town of Beiqiao in Puxi, so that all districts under the county can receive the benefits. There is nothing but joy. However, the district is far away from the Pujiang River. If there are strong winds and waves, it is inconvenient to cross the river. Moreover, it is more than twenty miles away from Beiqiao Town, making it difficult to reach after a long journey. If there is an acute illness, it will inevitably be too late to treat it, and there will still be the tragic scene of waiting for death. The district magistrate, seeing this, could not remain silent, so he dared to speak for the people, requesting that your excellency treat everyone equally and approve the forwarding of a letter to the Public Shanghai Hospital, requesting that it also establish a branch hospital in the fifth district, so as to popularize it and care for the lives of the people, which would be a public virtue and convenient for both sides.

Child Dies After Mother Feeds Opium Dregs for Diarrhea; Police Charge Mother with Murder 103

Yao Ma, the wife of local coppersmith Yao Quan'gen, who lives at No. 14, Lane 68, Rue du Père Robert, in the French Concession, on the previous day, because her ten-month-old son Xinglin suffered from persistent diarrhea, sought opium dregs at home and fed them to the child with boiling water in the hope of curing the disease. Unexpectedly, he swallowed an excessive amount and was poisoned. He was sent to the hospital, but the treatment was ineffective. He died that evening. The hospital reported to the police station, who took the child's body to the autopsy room. After the court confirmed the autopsy, the body was collected for burial. As reported in yesterday's newspaper, the police station believes that the child's mother, Yao Ma, was ignorant and, instead of seeking medical treatment, rashly fed the child the poisonous opium dregs, causing his death. For the criminal responsibility she should bear for homicide, and to warn ignorant women in general to prevent future occurrences, a detective was specially dispatched to arrest Yao Ma and send her to the Second Special District Court for investigation yesterday. At 2:30 PM, the criminal division chief Wang Kaixu presided over the interrogation in the first criminal court. First, the police lawyer Fei Xizhen explained the case and prosecuted according to Article 291 of the Criminal Code. Yao Ma confessed that the deceased was her own son, Xinglin. Because he had diarrhea, it gradually became severe. She heard people say that opium dregs could stop diarrhea, so she sought them and fed them to the child, but unexpectedly, it caused a great disaster. She begged for leniency. The court verified the confession and ordered that the announcement of the verdict be postponed. The defendant was returned to custody to await further instructions.

Three People Attempt Suicide Due to Inability to Make a Living 111

Elderly, Middle-Aged, and Young: Jumping into the Huangpu River One After Another

Representing Three Stages... Worthy of Attention

Although All Were Rescued... Efforts Should Be Made for Aftercare

Recently, there have been frequent cases of people committing suicide by jumping into the Huangpu River due to negative views. Yesterday, three more men jumped into the river to end their lives. Fortunately, all were rescued. The reasons are mostly due to economic pressure, leading them to this end. The details are recorded below:

Doddery Old Man

At 8:00 AM yesterday, a doddery old man suddenly jumped into the Huangpu River at the Lan Nidu Ferry in Pudong when others were not paying attention. The pier police officer immediately discovered this and directed nearby ferrymen to rescue him. He was taken to the Third District and identified as Zhang Wenmin, 61 years old, from Hunan. He recently came to Shanghai from his hometown by boat, but was unsuccessful in finding a job that his friends promised to get him. His travel expenses were exhausted, and he had no means of living, so he had to sacrifice his old life to avoid becoming a starving ghost. He was in tears, and his condition was extremely pitiful. A suicide note was found next to him, stating that he was committing suicide due to environmental pressure and requesting that if anyone retrieved his body, they should collect it on his behalf. The district magistrate ordered him to be sent to the General Bureau for Relief.

Robust Young Man

At 10:00 AM yesterday, a robust young man hired a sampan at the French Concession Company Wharf, stating that he was going to the Longmao Wharf in Pudong. When they arrived at Pudongxin, he suddenly jumped into the water to end his life. The sampan man quickly rescued him and sent him to the Customs Water Police Station. He identified himself as Li Dezhong, 24 years old, from Fuyang. He had been unemployed in his hometown for a long time, so he obtained some travel expenses and came to Shanghai to seek work. However, for three consecutive days, he had no place to live, and his travel expenses were exhausted. He had no face to return home, so he became disillusioned with the world. He said that he had a friend in Shanghai, living on Da Minguo Road. The police chief immediately sent someone to take him to his friend's place for relief.

Middle-Aged Man

At 1:30 PM yesterday, a middle-aged man boarded the Kunshan Maru, a small head ferry of the Nissin Company, at the Wuma Road Wharf, seemingly heading to Pudong. Unexpectedly, when the ship was heading south near Xiaodongmen on the Huangpu River, the man jumped into the raging waves to end his life. Fortunately, the old boatman Miao Sheng discovered him, and the ship immediately turned around and sailed back to rescue him. Seeing that the man's body sank and floated again, he used a bamboo pole to hook him onto the ship and sent him to the Customs Water Police Station. It was observed that he had scabies and was very smelly. When asked about the reason for his suicide, he said that his name was Zhao Zuguang, 31 years old, from Ningbo. He used to work at the Gold Exchange, but due to bad friends, he gradually became depraved and lost his job. Recently, he has also been suffering from sores and lodging in a small inn in Mantingfang. His finances are becoming increasingly difficult, and his illness cannot be cured. He thinks that there is no interest in being a human being, and it is better to die early. He has a mother and an older brother, and his wife has passed away. The police chief ordered that his relatives be notified to take him home.

China Chemical Industry Society Hosts Chrysanthemum Garden Tour Group 112

Overthrow the Poppy, Which Harms the Country and the People

Promote Pyrethrum, Which Enriches the Country and Benefits the People

In order to make the people understand the importance of the pyrethrum business and to arouse the interest of all sectors in planting, the China Chemical Industry Society specially invited people from all walks of life to Anlangdu the day before yesterday to visit the society's chrysanthemum garden. In one day, more than 400 people registered to join, which shows the interest of all sectors in the pyrethrum business.

The society also set up a cool shed in the farm, with soda, tea, and other refreshments. The guests were tired from the journey, and seeing the soda and tea, they all rushed to eat, which was a lively and interesting scene. It was already noon when they returned.

Report on the Shaanxi Disaster Investigation by the Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee 113

Over Three Million Disaster Victims

Rural Areas on the Verge of Extinction

Without Huge Sums of Money

This Extraordinary Disaster Cannot Be Saved

Will Benevolent and Charitable People Please Come Forward?

The drought in Shaanxi Province began in the first year of the Republic of China and has persisted for five years without relief. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented in history. Although the local Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee has repeatedly remitted funds for disaster relief, reports of the disaster continue to arrive like snowflakes. The committee deeply feels helpless and, on May 13th, dispatched Vice-Chairman Mr. Gu Jisheng, along with General Secretary Mr. Ou Yongkang, and others to Shaanxi for investigation. Mr. Gu and his party have recently returned to Shanghai and reported the disaster conditions as follows:

Historical Disaster Conditions: The province experienced a severe drought for three years starting in the 17th year of the Republic of China, resulting in vast stretches of barren land and no harvest. Farmers originally had scarce savings, and after three years, the situation became unmanageable. The disaster was most severe in the western region of Guanzhong, followed by the eastern region, and then northern Shaanxi. Initially, people could survive by eating grass roots and tree bark, but eventually, even these were exhausted, and countless people starved to death. Although there were disaster relief funds from various sources, the disaster was too severe and the funds were insufficient, like using a cup of water to put out a burning cartload of firewood, which was of no avail. According to investigations by the authorities, the number of disaster victims in the province crying out for food reached more than 3,345,000, accounting for three-fifths of the province's population. The so-called "mournful cries of refugees fill the land" truly describes the situation in Shaanxi.

This Year's Disaster Conditions

At the beginning of spring this year, another severe drought struck, and the wheat seedlings that had been planted were on the verge of dying. Fortunately, in the late spring of March, abundant rain fell, and the withering wheat seedlings revived and flourished. There was great hope for a summer harvest, which could slightly relieve the distress. Unexpectedly, at the end of April and beginning of May, just when the wheat ears were forming, fierce winds arrived, accompanied by flying stones and sand. The warm climate suddenly turned frigid, and repeated black frosts descended. Wherever the frost reached, the stems and leaves withered, and the glimmer of hope was extinguished once again. More than ten counties north of the Wei River still had no harvest. The farmers suffered this extraordinary hardship, and cries of disaster filled the roads. Unable to survive, some hanged themselves in the fields. Alas, how tragic!

The Tragic State of Rural Villages: The rural villages of Shaanxi Province were originally very prosperous. Since the great drought, not only have the rural villages gone bankrupt, but they have been virtually annihilated. Initially, there was hope that the coming year might bring a turn for the better and a bountiful harvest, so people endured death and waited. However, the drought in the coming years only worsened. After three or four years, many people died. While most starved to death, many also died from epidemics. During the summer, when epidemics broke out, when one person died, their body was left in the wild, and their clothes were stripped, causing the epidemic to spread uncontrollably. Entire families died from the plague, and such cases were numerous. Consequently, the young and strong fled in droves. In the severely affected areas now, there are often no more than five or six families in a village, and those who remain are on the verge of death. Selling people has become commonplace. Married women fetch only two yuan each, and unmarried women only thirteen yuan. Farm families have no possessions left. Once the people are gone, only the timber can still be exchanged for money. So, regardless of the consequences, they tear down houses and cut down trees to prolong their lives for a few more days. Farming tools are the lifeline of farmers, but they are forced to sell them at a low price. At present, in the city of Xi'an, shops selling old timber and old farm implements are everywhere. Therefore, even if there is no further drought in the summer and autumn this year, farmers will have no seeds or tools and will be unable to cultivate the land. The tragic state of the rural villages has reached such a point; it is truly a great calamity.

Severe Disaster, Insufficient Funds: The severity of the disaster is roughly as described above. Seeking to remedy the situation is extremely difficult. The first priority is to prolong the lives of those who have not yet died. Generally, two or three yuan per person can sustain them for a month or two. Although the cost is very low, there are so many disaster victims that it cannot be done without a large sum of money. The second priority is to purchase seeds and farm implements to enable the farmers to resume their work. Otherwise, even if heaven sends timely rain, the farmers can only sigh and lament. The disaster area is extraordinarily vast, and it cannot be handled without a large sum of money. While in Xi'an, Mr. Gu and his party urgently telegraphed the committee to remit 10,000 yuan to purchase farm implements on a large scale to alleviate the immediate crisis. However, such a small amount is of little help. It is hoped that benevolent and charitable people will generously donate funds and pool together a large sum. Only then can the disaster in Shaanxi be slightly alleviated, and the hope for the survival of the people of Shaanxi will not be extinguished.

Jinghui Canal Project: Shaanxi Province has a high terrain, and its water conservancy is poorly maintained. The livelihood of the farmers depends entirely on the heavens. If it does not rain, death is certain. However, forests are scarce, and the existing trees are cut down without replanting. The possibility of rainfall decreases with each passing day. A certain Westerner predicted that Shaanxi Province might turn into a desert in the future. While this may not be entirely credible, it is not without reason for concern. The fundamental solution is to construct water conservancy projects to ensure irrigation for farmland. This is why the Jinghui Canal project is so important. At present, the Jinghui Canal project is 80-90% complete, irrigating over a million mu of farmland. However, the original plan to open up various branch canals, if successfully completed, would irrigate three to four million mu more than the existing canal. Now, due to a shortage of funds, it is impossible to proceed. Some people have contacted the Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee to request funds to undertake the construction of branch canals, which would cost approximately 100,000 yuan. The committee is not without the intention to undertake this, but the funds are not yet secured. It remains to be seen whether they can be raised, and it also relies on philanthropists to have compassion for this great disaster and donate large sums of money.

Acknowledgement: We received from The Commercial Press a complimentary copy each of The Eastern Miscellany, Volume 30, No. 11, The English Weekly, No. 34, Children's World, Volume 30, No. 11, and Children's Pictorial, No. 15. Thank you.

Weather Report 114

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The Shandong coast will be sunny, with winds from the southwest to northwest. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River will be cloudy with fog or rain, with winds from the southeast to northeast, but the weather will gradually clear during the day. The coastal area south of Ma'anshan Island and the East Sea will be cloudy with cyclone rain due to a small low pressure system passing through, moving eastward or east-northeastward. Furthermore, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the local area was 75.6 degrees and the lowest was 65.5 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 75.6 degrees and the lowest was 56.1 degrees.

Revised Customs Tariff Schedule (11) 115

Effective May 22nd

Class 12: Wood, Bamboo, Rattan, Straw, and Their Products. The term "light wood" in this class refers to various coniferous and acicular trees, such as pine, fir, cypress, larch, cedar, umbrella pine, juniper, and Japanese cypress. Broad-leaved trees are referred to as "heavy wood."

The English cubic foot measurement of lumber shall be based on the actual cubic volume of the wood.

The volume of round timber shall be calculated based on the diameter at the midpoint.

Reader Advisory

Seeking Education or Joining the Military 116

Reply to Mr. Zhou Minan of Shaoxing

Answer: The answers to the two questions you asked are as follows: (1) Given your difficult circumstances and inability to make ends meet, it is logically difficult to have the opportunity to pursue education. However, this is based on general circumstances. If you can truly utilize your environment, you can seek education anytime and anywhere, without necessarily having to enter middle school or university. The youth who attend middle school and university are mostly the children of middle-class or higher families. A poor youth like you naturally has no place among them. However, precisely because of this, the knowledge and education acquired by the children of the poor are exceptionally rich in content. For example, a poor child who knows the suffering of not being able to study due to lack of money can thus realize that, in order to enable all poor children to have access to education, it is necessary to work hard to transform the social roots of poverty. Or, for example, a poor child who has seen and personally experienced the exploitation by local tyrants, evil gentry, corrupt officials, and bureaucrats in the countryside can thus realize that, in order to relieve farmers from suffering, it is necessary to fundamentally transform the rural areas. All of these are knowledge and education that middle school and university students can never obtain in classrooms or books. In a period of great change, the cultural level of the people, especially the cultural level of revolutionaries, cannot be measured by school education but must be assessed by the progressive course of their social life. Having said this, I want to encourage you to take heart. You are capable of seeking education, but this kind of learning is not to be sought in schools but in the daily struggles of social life. This is the first question. (2) "Pingjin is in danger." Instead of committing suicide, it is better to join the military. This approach can be taken under the following conditions: First, the organizers and commanders of this army, as well as their usual education and training, must truly possess a revolutionary spirit of anti-imperialism and national defense, and they must have resolute action. Second, otherwise, the person joining the military must have deep foresight, loyalty, courage, and steadfastness, what is called "leaving the easy for the difficult," what is called "entangling roots and intertwined branches." If the army you join can truly resolutely resist, then you may charge into the enemy, die generously, use your blood to resist foreign enemies, and awaken the national soul. If the army you join is not a revolutionary army but flees at the sight of the enemy, then you must unite the people and fight to the death with the invading army of imperialists. The heroic and great education given to us by the citizens of Paris in 1871 is clearly visible. Even if you are crushed to pieces, you can die with your eyes closed in peace. However, now that the North has already negotiated a ceasefire and is carrying out a peace movement, you can temporarily calm your anger. I also hope that you will think calmly, open your eyes and look at the facts, and do not needlessly go to your death in vain!

Education News

Important News: Wang Shijie Discusses the Problem of Education Finance Reform 117

Proposed Inheritance Tax to Fund Education

Education Finance Independent Management Committee

(Nanjing, 1st) Wang Shijie stated that, regarding the problem of education finance reform, after repeated consultations with the central government, principles have now been formulated. First, regarding the confirmation of income, in addition to the existing funds, it is proposed to levy an inheritance tax to be transferred to education expenses. Second, regarding the independence of education finance, it is proposed to establish an Education Finance Management Committee to be specifically responsible for this matter. These principles will be submitted to the Central Political Council for discussion and decision after being agreed upon by the various committees of the central government.

Ministry of Education to Merge Departments of Shanxi College of Arts and Law 118

(Nanjing, 1st) In order to reorganize higher education in Shanxi, the Ministry of Education has ordered the Shanxi Provincial Department of Education to merge duplicate departments. Starting from the next academic year, the Provincial College of Education and the Provincial College of Law should be merged into Shanxi University. The three departments of the College of Education will be merged into the College of Arts of Shanxi University, and the two departments of the College of Law will be merged into the College of Law of Shanxi University. The funds of the two colleges will be allocated to Shanxi University, totaling more than 430,000 yuan annually. With more ample funds, various facilities can be easily established. Books and instruments will be uniformly merged, making it easier to achieve complete equipment. Faculty and staff will be reassigned duties, ensuring that everyone is qualified and competent. Then, the administrative organization will be simplified to the greatest extent, and the savings will be used to enrich the content. By concentrating all efforts on this, it will be easier to achieve perfection. As for the science and medical departments, Shanxi University will gradually plan to add them according to its economic situation.

Local News

Health Education Exhibition Opened Yesterday

- More than 10,000 exhibits on display in two venues, a feast for the eyes

- Mayor Wu speaks of the need for Chinese people to overcome the mentality of relying on heaven for sustenance

- Children's dental health competition to be held during the exhibition

The first Health Education Exhibition, co-sponsored by the Shanghai Municipal Education and Health Bureaus, opened yesterday at the Puyi Society and Cangji Primary School venues. The opening ceremony was held at the Puyi Society at 10:00 am. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives: In addition to Chairman Wu Tiecheng, Vice-Chairmen Pan Gongzhan and Li Tingan, and all members of the Health Education Committee, representatives from various organizations included Cao Peizi from the Municipal Party Department, Li Dachao from the Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center, Liu Yide from the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Zhu Jiqing from the National Health Administration, Wu Liande from the Maritime Quarantine Service, Xu Yiheng from the Garrison Command, Xiao Qixiong from the Public Security Bureau, Pan Hongding from the Municipal Council, Zhu Shaoping from the World Student Service, Lu Bokui from the Library Association, Sun Choucheng from the New Drug Association, and more than 500 teachers and students from various schools.

Venue Situation: Along the Zhonghua Road area from Xiaonanmen to Dadongmen, there were large white cloth banners across the street. Above the entrance of the venue hung a bright banner that read "To strengthen the country, one must first strengthen the body; physical education and hygiene are the methods." In addition to the Public Security Bureau dispatching police to maintain order, Zhou Mingshi led the entire Boy Scout troop of Junyi Middle School to maintain order at the first venue. The Upper China Experimental Primary School Boy Scouts provided services at the second venue. A Red Cross Hospital ambulance was stationed at the venue for protection. Therefore, although attendance was very enthusiastic yesterday, the order was well maintained. The opening ceremony was held at the performance area of the first venue.

Opening Ceremony: The ceremony was held at 10:00 am, presided over by Chairman Wu Tiecheng, recorded by Yu Wenwei, and emceed by Peng Quji. After the customary rites, Mayor Wu delivered an address, followed by reports from the two Bureau Chiefs, Pan and Li, on the preparations. Finally, guests such as Wu Liande, Director of the Maritime Quarantine Service, and Zhu Jiqing from the National Health Administration, gave speeches successively. The meeting adjourned for a photo session at around 11:00 am.

Mayor's Address: Mayor Wu's address briefly stated: "Gentlemen, today is the first Health Education Exhibition held in Shanghai. Most of those attending the ceremony are young students, which shows that Chinese youth are paying close attention to health education. Mr. Sun Yat-sen said, 'We Chinese rely on heaven for sustenance.' This sentence sums up the major problem of China's weakness and decline over the past century. A Chinese proverb also says, 'If the King of Hell wants you dead by the third watch, you cannot escape it.' It entrusts the misfortunes, diseases, and sufferings of our lives, and even the rise and fall of the country, to fate, as if there is a master god controlling our entire lives. As a result, various undertakings in China have been affected by the mentality of relying on heaven for sustenance in the past eighty or ninety years. This time, the Japanese are oppressing China with military force and occupying our territory. Old Chinese ideas say that this is the country's destiny, entrusting the fate of the country to heaven, so that the inherent strength of people is not fully expressed, resulting in the decline of various undertakings in China. This is the most dangerous phenomenon, and it is also what those who are devoted to saving the country are very distressed about and want to find a way to overcome this idea. We believe that a person has the power to resist our environment and control our lives, but the most important thing is health. The strength of our bodies and the length of our lives are all man-made and not reliant on heaven. One should first seek one's own health. The key to the success of great entrepreneurs, great politicians, and great thinkers throughout history, both Chinese and foreign, lies in their health surpassing ordinary people. Therefore, if we want the success of personal and public undertakings, we must first seek health. To seek one's own health, in addition to receiving sufficient health education and hygienic knowledge, we must also overcome the old idea of relying on heaven for sustenance. The fate of China, the fate of the Chinese nation, and the fate of each of us are all in our own hands and not reliant on heaven. You are all young students, and the future responsibility of China lies on your shoulders, so you should pay attention to your health now and prepare to shoulder the great responsibility of the country in the future."

Bureau Chiefs' Reports: Bureau Chief Pan of the Education Bureau reported briefly that the Health Education Exhibition held today is only one type of health education activity in this year. This event is organized by the Health Education Committee and is divided into two major parts: exhibition and performance. The exhibition is divided into school, society, and reference groups. The school exhibits are all from municipal and registered private primary and secondary schools. Twenty-four municipal schools were designated to participate, and more than 180 schools participated freely. There are nine middle schools. In the social group, in addition to schools, social organizations also participated. The reference group is for exhibits specifically for research. In total, there are more than 12,000 exhibits participating in this exhibition. Due to the excessive number of exhibits, a second venue has been added at Cangji Primary School. In terms of performance, there are various children's health activities, and the Health Bureau is responsible for various tasks such as bathing, vaccination, and dental check-ups for children. The significance of this exhibition is not just to complete the exhibition once, but to enable all those who attend to understand its significance and pay attention to personal and public hygiene, said Bureau Chief Pan. Bureau Chief Li of the Health Bureau reported briefly that the two words "health" are closely related to individuals and the country. The Health Education Exhibition is organized by the Education and Health Bureaus under the guidance of the Mayor. It was established on February 1 and is now beginning to exhibit after preparations. Its significance is very important. I hope that after the citizens of this city visit, they will put the images they have gained into practice. This is indeed the first time it has been held in Shanghai. In addition to hoping that it will be held annually, we also hope that a large-scale national exhibition will be held in the future, he said.

Guests' Speeches: Zhu Jiqing, the representative of the Ministry of Interior's Health Department, said briefly that public health is progressing very quickly in countries around the world, but they are all proceeding by using laws or improving the environment. However, in practice, there are various difficulties. Laws cannot control personal hygiene, and the environment cannot be improved. Therefore, everyone is now thinking of starting from the aspect of education. Since the sixteenth year of the Republic, health undertakings and health movements have been publicized a lot in China, but health requires practice, not formality. In addition to the exhibition, this exhibition also has vaccination and other work, which is to seek knowledge on the one hand and practice on the other, he said. Finally, Wu Liande, Director of the Maritime Quarantine Service, gave a speech.

Dental Competition: In order to promote oral hygiene and make citizens pay attention to dental health, the association held an internal dental health competition. All children under the age of fourteen can participate. The regulations stipulate that the inspection time is from 9:00 am to 5:00 pm every day during the exhibition. After the dentist has completed the inspection, the top three with the healthiest teeth will be awarded prizes by the Family Industry Society. The first place winner will receive twenty-four kinds of prizes, the second place winner sixteen kinds, and the third place winner eight kinds. The bottom three with the worst teeth will receive free treatment. Those who participated in the competition yesterday were quite enthusiastic. The inspection dates are still today and tomorrow.

Today's Program: 9:00 to 10:00 am Human Pyramid Singing Health Stories (Meixi), Boy Soldiers (Jingye Attached Elementary School). 10:00 to 11:00 am Expressive Song Beat Down the Enemy (Xiangde), The Doctor's Words (Shuji), Health Activities Disease Vectors (Danhua). 1:00 to 2:00 pm The Harm of Mosquitoes and Flies Health Performance (Tangwan), Student Soldiers Dirty Children (Wanzhu). 2:00 to 4:00 pm Lecture on Health Knowledge for Teachers and Staff. 4:00 to 5:00 pm Various Health Performances (Liangjiang).

The Heude Museum Will Open 122

Starting next Monday

The animal and plant sections will be opened first

The Zi Lin Daily reported that the Heude Museum of Aurora University on Luba Road will open a portion of its collection to the public for viewing starting next Monday. The rest is also expected to open soon. The part that will be opened this time is the animal and plant section. The admission fee is two dimes per person. Viewing hours are from 2:00 pm to 5:00 pm every day except Tuesdays. The museum was originally the Xujiahui Museum, founded in 1883. In 1931, it was moved to the French Concession and merged into Aurora University. It was named after the founder Heude. The collection of animal and plant specimens is extremely rich. In addition to China, there are also animals and plants from Japan, the Philippines, Vietnam, Siam, Java, and Malacca. The section on bronze and stone artifacts is also expected to open soon.

Eight Records Broken in the Preliminary Competition

Special Feature

Recent Reforms in Curriculum and Educational Administration in Soviet Russian Primary and Secondary Schools (II) by Zhu Zhensun 140

3. Improvements in Teaching and Training Work

Since the passage of the Improved Curriculum Plan on September 5, 1931, there has been significant progress in the teaching work in primary and secondary schools. Although the Central Committee ordered all schools not to adopt any method as the basic teaching method, in practice many schools had adopted the so-called forced group experimental teaching method. As a result, not only was the teacher's task reduced to an extremely low level, but also the individual work of each student was neglected. Therefore, the Central Committee of the Soviet Russian Communist Party requested the education committees of all Soviet republics to correct the errors produced by this method and reorganize the teaching work in schools according to the following principles:

(1) Primary and secondary schools should uniformly adopt the recitation method in the classroom. This recitation should be based on the subjects scheduled in the curriculum and the specified number of students. This teaching method can be used in both group and individual teaching.

(2) Teachers should train students to use textbooks in a systematic way. They should also encourage students to work independently in study rooms, laboratories, and discussion groups. They should lead students to visit factories, museums, farms, forests, and other places. When they are preparing to help students solve difficult problems, they should encourage them to work independently on solving problems, writing essays, building models, conducting experiments, and collecting materials. The Central Committee of the Communist Party also granted educational personnel the privilege of leading school work.

(3) Each student's individual work record can be used as a basis for academic performance. Teachers should conduct a detailed study of each student, and at the end of each semester, he must prepare a report card for each student in each specified subject. At the end of each academic year, all students must participate in the general examination.

(4) The Education Committee should prescribe various training work and appropriate methods for working in laboratories, farms, and factories suitable for students' ages in the shortest possible time.

(5) In the past, school administrators and teachers did not pay attention to the problem of disrupting school order, nor did they make efforts to promote organized training. But now the principals and teachers in schools should bear major responsibility for maintaining discipline in schools. For this purpose, they must cooperate with social organizations, students' parents, and the Communist Youth League pioneers. Students who insult teachers, violate school regulations, and destroy school property should be expelled and have no right to return to school for one to three years.

(6) The Education Committee should prescribe various systematic educational propaganda methods and publish them in various educational publications in the shortest possible time.

(7) Because the effectiveness of school work mostly depends on material equipment, such as instruments in laboratories, tools in industrial rooms, and other teaching aids, the Education Committee must prepare a budget for the equipment that primary and secondary schools should have within two months in order to proceed with the purchase.

4. Teachers

(1) In the past few years, since the Central Committee of the Communist Party recognized the growing activities and increased responsibilities of teachers, attention has been paid to the task of teachers. The greatest task of Soviet Russian teachers should be to impart basic scientific knowledge to students and cultivate their respect for discipline and a socialist attitude towards reading and work. The Central Committee of the Communist Party requested that the Education Committees of all Soviet republics and other party and government organs, within their powers, should provide teachers with convenience so that they can fulfill the task of cultivating and educating Soviet youth. At present, the political status of teachers has been raised, their teaching skills are being improved in every possible way, and they have been granted the same rights as workers in factories in terms of purchasing food, clothing, salary payments, housing, daily needs, and entertainment.

(2) When the Education Committee newly appoints or transfers teachers, it should encourage experienced teachers to help inexperienced teachers. Any local agency must not force teachers to engage in other social work during the time they are teaching, attending continuing education, or participating in special school meetings, and they must absolutely not be used as messengers.

(3) The children of teachers should have the same rights as the children of workers when they enter higher education institutions.

(4) Starting in January 1933, the Soviet Russian National Publishing Department began compiling and publishing a selected collection of educational books for teachers to refer to at low prices.

(5) The Education Committee should plan the steps for its implementation in the shortest possible time for teacher training work (including correspondence courses and crash courses). This training work should pay special attention to working methods and cultivating the ability to use maps, instruments, charts, radios, and other teaching aids. As for measures to reward teachers with outstanding achievements, they are also being actively planned. (End)

Free Talk

Scolding and Praising 141

— Zhou Muzhai

Writing is a weapon of literary criticism. If used properly, it can be an immortal achievement. If used improperly, it often invites criticism of the weapon itself. Usage is not the same as grammar. "Writing is born from nature, and a masterpiece is achieved by chance." Chinese writers have always looked down on grammar. The beauty lies in the word "chance."

Writing has a "literary mind," and a "skillful hand" must first be able to "understand the heart." Satire is not as good as praise, and denigration is not as good as commendation. Praising the dead is not as good as praising the living. These are the so-called "literary mind." However, praise has its own reasoning. For example, if you flatter someone on the wrong foot, you will end up working hard and not pleasing anyone. Han Fei wrote the "Saying Difficulty" chapter, and Mr. Guigu also had the art of vertical and horizontal strategy, which shows the importance and prudence of the ancients in praising others.

In ancient times, writers were best at praising. Since the change of dynasty, the "literary mind" has changed greatly, so modern writers have all taken scolding as their ability. Those who restore the old scold the declining world, those who pursue the new scold the accumulation of problems, the steady scold the excessive, and the radical scold the conservative. There is scolding in the writing, and no writing outside of scolding. However, praising is already difficult, and scolding is even more difficult. The reason why national affairs are difficult to discuss today is because everyone wants to scold.

The same scolding, scolding the near is not as good as scolding the far. The same scolding, scolding can contrast with praise. If you can "understand the heart," then you have a "skillful hand." For example, people near the center can scold the southeast, southwest, northeast, and northwest. People in the southeast, southwest, northeast, and northwest can also exclude their own location and scold the distant places like the people in the center. This way of avoiding the real and attacking the empty allows the scolder to feel happy, and the scolded person cannot hear it, or has no way to do anything even if they hear it. Scolding and not scolding are exactly the same. Otherwise, scolding people to their faces will surely suffer an immediate loss. How could there be such a fool in the world? Also, some people who are endowed with the "right to scold" can scold A sometimes and scold B sometimes. But like Jiao Da in the Dream of the Red Chamber, he scolded everyone in the Ning and Rong families, but the pair of stone lions in front of the door were clean. This way of attacking the east and striking the west turns scolding into praise. Openly praising people, how could there be such a fool in the world? Then, is today's "literary mind" not better than the ancient "literary mind"?

Passing Seven 142

— Lin Weiyin

Alone in the room, everything inside and outside is silent, but I don't want to sleep or read, but I have to do something, otherwise the silence that is approaching step by step will make it difficult to breathe. When I am almost unable to resolve this, I often helplessly think of "passing seven."

As soon as I get a deck of cards, my heart calms down, as if the head of a chased pheasant has found its hiding place. While turning the cards one by one, I hope, expect, care, and worry. Seeing that a black seven and a black nine have been turned out, how I yearn for a red eight to be turned out. When it really turns out, it feels as comfortable as drinking a sip of mellow wine. If it doesn't turn out, I quickly shift my hope to the next card. Hope continues like this, and it is also a little tense. And from this, it seems that being a human being is not entirely meaningless.

Until I finally see clearly that this time I will not be able to "pass seven," I shuffle the cards and start again. While shuffling the cards, I think annoyed: If only a black jack came! If only a diamond three came!

It is the beginning of a new situation.

This time it is very smooth, and almost everything I want comes. So I am pleased. So I am happy.

But suddenly, I think, repeatedly, how is it that I am going to "pass" this time! This time it will really "pass"! So panic takes the place of joy. Because after passing once, I will not have the perseverance to pass a second time. The more I see that I will pass, the more the area of panic expands.

I really "passed"! The silence that had temporarily left rushes back from all around without hesitation.

So I am again trapped in the middle of silence.

Before Dawn 143

— Zhang Tingzheng

Before Dawn:

Big city --

Black smoke, bursting straight from the chimneys! Whistles, toot-toot, Hysteria's wild howl!

Blue-clad ranks, diffuse, diffuse, diffuse the streets: surging, this angry tide, this human tide! Crude, angry, the threat of death, the lure of light! This whistle, like a signal, the black night falls! The white day arrives! People! Laughing madly!

On the other side of the city --

Red and green Neons are extinguished! Jazz, tango, cease, quiet. Young masters, young ladies, drunkenly, heavily, lie like corpses in the arms of men and women, accompanying the night god to the black country!

An aunt, lazily, drags the opium-scorched old master, saying: It's almost dawn, why don't you go to sleep!

Before Dawn:

Big Village --

The warm moonlight rolls away! The beautiful stars also hide one by one! Light mixed in the fog, people suffocate, can't breathe, the sky seems faint! But, before dawn there is always a section of fog, light will expand from the fog, forcing the fog so that there is not even a shadow! Look, that east, has revealed a line of red light! Ah! Really!

Old man, little grandson, big son, a large group! Hoes, plows, shovels, shouldered on tattered clothes; old, young, all laughing happily, toward the direction of the sunrise, bravely, calmly, walking! Running!

On the other side of the village --

An old, large house with a garden of flowers and trees, on a nanmu bed, a sick old man, sitting and panting. Beside him, a woman in her thirties, wearing black silk clothes, worried, sad!

"Niang of Shen'er! I!! I'm afraid I won't last long! But, I can't rest easy! The times have changed, the harvest is worse year after year, the tenants are more and more arrogant every day, and now they are even unwilling to pay the rent! Alas! In this world, the gentry is afraid of not being able to survive! You, mother and son..." The old man gasped heavily, unable to say the words that followed.

Before Dawn:

In the market town!!

Vegetable vendors, rickshaw pullers, the dregs of the city! Each, each, preparing, climbing out of bed!

Ah! Noisy, chaotic, rows of rickshaws, loads of vegetables, swarms of people!

In the dim light, they appear to be struggling!

On the other side of the market town!!

In a front building upstairs, a young man with disheveled hair and a torn suit, his face a mixture of anger and sorrow, sitting on a three-legged stool, facing the unfinished teapot,

"It's over. All the methods are over! The clothes are pawned! The things are sold! There's no place to borrow money, and I can't find a job! What generations of scholars, what status; bookishness, status doesn't give us food to eat! Go! Go! We go down! Down to……

Random Musings from Qu Lu 144

— Zi Zhan

(39) The Origin of Couplets

Those who discuss楹聯 (Ying Lian, pillar couplets) have always believed that they originated with the peach wood charms that Meng Chang of the Later Shu kingdom inscribed himself:

"New Year welcomes abundant blessings,

Auspicious festival marks everlasting spring."

When I read Li Yishan's collected works, in the first half of his poem "Returning to Prefect Pei Mingfu's Residence," where he says, "That person chose a secluded and deep place to build, the cinnamon alleys and cedar paths are impossible to find. On the pillars are carved couplets, in the troughs the horses tilt their heads to listen to the zither," I strongly suspected that the phrase "pillars with carved characters" refers to楹聯 (Ying Lian, pillar couplets), not insect borings or traces. Later, I read the "Biography of Lu Yun" in the Book of Jin, which records that Yun met with Xun Yin and sat with Zhang Hua. Hua said, "Today we meet, let's not engage in commonplace talk." Yun then raised his hand and said,

"Lu Shilong of the Lu family from the clouds."

Yin replied,

"Xun Minghe of the Xun family under the sun."

Minghe was Yin's courtesy name. I also read the "Biography of Xi Zuochi," which records that the Buddhist monk Shi Dao'an of the Sangha order was intelligent, eloquent, and highly talented. When he arrived in Jingzhou from the north and first met Zuochi, Dao'an said,

"Shi Dao'an who fills the sky."

Zuochi said,

"Xi Zuochi of the four seas."

People at the time considered it a famous pairing. It can be seen that during the Jin Dynasty, refined discussions and spoken language also valued parallelism and elegance. However, this can be called spoken couplets, which are not the same as the pillar couplets that later generations refer to. Spoken couplets are used to display eloquence, while pillar couplets emphasize decoration. The former came before the latter, and there is a clear trace of transition to be found. Our country's characters are monosyllabic and isolated. They have tones that can be modulated to create euphony, and they have radicals that reveal their shapes. Odd and even numbers are generated in tandem, capturing the wonders of nature; low and high tones alternate, vying for the marvels of the sounds of nature. The Book of Documents has the saying, "Arrogance invites loss, while humility receives benefit," and poetry has the line, "Seeing much misfortune, one receives no small amount of insult." When human culture first emerged, language was also occasionally parallel. As artistic expression gradually developed, rhetoric became increasingly beautiful. This is why, between the Han and Wei dynasties, writing tended to strive for the path of 整膽 (zheng dan, a style characterized by parallelism and balanced structure). If we want to investigate the origin of couplets, we must know that first, there was writing that admired parallelism; second, spoken language also valued parallelism; and then, there were parallel pillar couplets, used as decorative tools.

Correction

Yesterday's "Random Musings from Qu Lu" (38) was mistakenly labeled (37). Also, in the line "Returning ten years to make a prisoner," "ten years" was mistakenly printed as "ten years." This is hereby corrected.

Carrot Top 145

— Julcs　kenarn, written by, Lin Qu, translated

Selected Correspondence between Carrot Top and His Father (Continued)

Carrot Top to Mr. Lepic:

Dear Father,

I have delivered your wild rabbit to our history and geography teacher, Mr. Legris. I think this gift certainly made him very happy. He repeatedly asked me to thank you on his behalf. When I entered, carrying a wet umbrella, he personally took it from my hand and placed it by the door. Then we chatted casually. He told me that if I worked hard, I could get first place in history and geography at the end of the year. But you can imagine that while we were talking, I was standing the whole time, and Mr. Legris didn't even offer me a seat? But other than that, he was very kind.

Is this negligence or arrogance?

I can't come to a conclusion, dear Father, and I'd really like to hear your opinion.

Mr. Lepic's reply:

Dear Carrot Top,

You're never satisfied. Mr. Gide asked you to sit down, and you were dissatisfied. Mr. Legris let you stand, and you're still dissatisfied. Perhaps you're not old enough to demand that others show you respect. Mr. Legris may not have offered you a seat, but you can forgive him; it must be because you're so small that he mistakenly thought you were sitting down.

Carrot Top to Mr. Lepic:

Dear Father,

I hear you're going to Paris. I want to share in all the joy you experience traveling in the capital. This is a place I really want to admire and would be happiest to go with you. I know that schoolwork won't allow me to go with you, but I'm taking this opportunity to ask you for something: I don't know if you could buy me a book or two. I've already read all the books I have now thoroughly. Please choose a book or two as you see fit. Actually, any book will do. But what I want most is Voltaire's "Henriade" and Rousseau's "Nouvelle Héloïse." If you bring me these two books (books in Paris are extremely cheap), I can swear to you that the supervisor will definitely not confiscate them.

Mr. Lepic's reply:

Dear Carrot Top,

Those writers you mentioned are just like you and me. What they wrote, you can do too. You can write a few books yourself, and then read them yourself.

Mr. Lepic to Carrot Top:

Dear Carrot Top,

The letter I received from you this morning astonished me greatly. I read it several times, but I still don't understand it. This is not your usual writing style, and in that letter, you said some strange things that, as I see it, neither you nor I can understand.

Usually, you always tell us your trivial matters, you tell us your grades in school, the advantages or disadvantages you've discovered in each teacher, the names of your new classmates, the condition of all your clothes, how well you sleep and eat, etc.

These are the things I care about. But today, I'm completely baffled. Please tell me, since we're in the middle of winter now, why are you talking about a spring outing? What does this mean? Do you need a scarf? Your letter doesn't have a date written on it, and it doesn't even say whether you're writing to me or to a dog. Even your handwriting seems to have changed, and the line breaks and the number of capital letters are all incomprehensible to me. In short, you seem to be mocking someone. I guess you're mocking yourself, not someone else. I don't want to give you a demerit now, but I'm giving you a warning.

Carrot Top's reply:

Dear Father,

I'm very busy now, and I can only give you one sentence to explain the letter I sent you last time. Didn't you realize that the letter was written in "rhyme"?

Silk Cocoon News Snippets

Jinhua Silk Harvest Only 20-30% The new cocoons of the Jinhua prefecture were launched on the market earlier than those of Hangzhou and Shaoxing. This year, due to weather damage, the silk harvest only reached 20-30%. The cocoon market has been open for over ten days, but the recent arrival of goods is sparse, and preparations are being made to close the market. Cocoon prices are as high as 32-33 yuan and as low as 25-26 yuan.

Scarce New Cocoons from Liuxia Fetch High Prices In the Liuxia area of Hangzhou, the cocoon production is not abundant this year. Many farmers are raising local breeds. The cocoon market has been open for more than a week. In the past two days, the arrival of goods has become even scarcer, and cocoon prices are high in spring. Each market has insufficient goods. Superior foreign breed cocoons are priced at 37-38 yuan.

Xindai Foreign Breed Cocoons are of the Highest Quality In Huzhou's Xindai, silkworm rearing was not smooth this year, and both local and foreign breeds were raised. Cocoon production is not abundant. The foreign breed cocoons are of the highest quality. Cocoon merchants are vying to purchase them, and the cocoon price has risen from 34-35 yuan to 40 yuan.

Few Superior Cocoons in Yucheng, Prices Not High Most farmers are raising local breeds, resulting in poor harvests and quality. After the cocoon market opened, the cocoons were of poor quality. Merchants from Huai and Wei were not interested, and the price opened at 24-25 to 27-28 yuan. Improved breed cocoons were priced at 32 yuan.

Few Cocoon Markets Open in Nanjing New cocoons from the surrounding countryside have been launched on the market. This year, most silkworm farmers are raising foreign breeds, with guidance from students of the Jin Da Silkworm Department. Cocoon production is still good. Unfortunately, only two or three cocoon markets, such as Minfeng, have opened. Cocoon prices are as high as 34-35 yuan and as low as 25-26 yuan.

The arrival of goods is still smooth, with selective purchasing. Foreign breed cocoons are priced at 33-34 yuan, and local breed cocoons at 25-26 yuan.

The weather is sunny and rainy, and it is unpredictable. The selling households are tight, and the market is tight. As for Zhejiang tung oil, it also affects the Han market. Therefore, although the market in each place has risen, it is also a temporary trend. Whether it can last depends on the real sales in each place.
