Spring and Autumn

Shanghai is Full of Gold 161

— Ying Zi

People in the mainland say that Shanghai is full of gold. Those who refute say that Shanghai's roads are paved with asphalt, or wooden blocks, or stone blocks. How can there be any gold? It's just a dream.

But this country bumpkin, who has been working as a three-story attic dweller in Shanghai for three years, feels that the ground is full of gold, and it is indeed not a dream.

Some Shanghai villagers inherited 20 or 30 acres of land from their fathers. Although younger brothers and typists divided the property, and sisters and nephews also came to nibble away at some of it, they still had five or six acres left, which they rented to people to build thirteen or fourteen-story buildings. Every ten or eight years, Shanghai became more and more prosperous, and land prices soared day by day, from 30,000 yuan per acre to 50,000 yuan to 100,000 yuan to 200,000 yuan. Is that not a gold mine?

This is speaking of the landowners. Even the proletariat can find some gold on the land.

At every tram stop, or at the entrance of public places, you can often see some proletarian comrades, one hand carrying a blue-green, white-not-white cloth bag, and the other hand carrying large bamboo chopsticks, picking up cigarette butts everywhere. They can sell them to exchange for pancakes, fried dough sticks, sorghum wine, earth leather, and cage water.

Every month, at the end of the month, after a heavy and desolate sound of selling long ingots, the pavilion aunts and three-story attic aunts gathered at the back gate, burning their way. At this time, the proletariat wielded brooms and dustpans together, like a whirlwind sweeping away the remnants of the clouds, euphemistically called collecting tinfoil ash. It is said that tinfoil ash is more valuable than cigarette butts.

There is also a kind of person who specializes in turning over garbage cans. Those who are experienced in this way say that picking up cigarette butts and collecting tinfoil ash is not very meaningful. Turning over garbage cans is the most interesting. In the garbage can, chicken feathers, meat bones, and everyday meals are common. Copper coins and silver coins are not rare. If you are lucky, you can find gold silk rings and gold rings. Haha, you don't need to thank you, and you don't need to be surprised.

Shanghai is full of gold. The villagers do not deceive me. In Shanghai, there is indeed a way to make a living.

Dai Jitao's Filial Piety is Unwavering 162

— Zheng Yimei

President Dai Jitao recently built a villa in the scenic area of Tangshan. There is a Buddhist hall in the villa, and the walls are engraved with his mother's handwritten Classic of Filial Piety to commemorate her. Dai was orphaned early and raised by his mother. She drew bears and taught him, not inferior to the mothers of Liu Zhongying and Ouyang Xiu in the history books. Dai was also able to follow filial piety in everything and listen only to his mother's instructions. He once engraved a chapter saying: "Hate fine wine." He often used it on letters and notes, because his mother thought that wine could disrupt the mind and told him not to get close to distiller's yeast. His mother was thrifty and set an example, and Dai was also able to maintain his frugality. When he was in charge of the People's Rights Newspaper, he often went to small restaurants in Wantingfang to fill his stomach. Even after he became noble and prominent, he still did not forget the flavor of the salted pork and tofu soup in the small restaurant. He often went to enjoy it. Occasionally, when he entertained guests at his residence, the dishes were always prepared by himself, with four bowls and one basin. The bowls were chicken claws, duck feet, pig feet, and sheep hooves, and the basin contained only two salted eggs, which he called the four-foot-one-egg banquet. He liked to eat peanuts to help his writing. When writing the declaration of the Fifth Plenary Session, according to his attendants, he ate 480 peanuts. His populism was like this.

His mother's calligraphy was beautiful and she was good at poetry. She had a poem crying for Master Xiaoxuan: Alas, Master, you have gone to study literature. I wanted to follow you, but my son held me back. The eldest son has grown up, and the youngest has not yet grown up. Even if the mother teaches, how can it be like the father? Alas! Morning after morning, dawn after dusk, life and death are both sad. The loving mother is old and her heart is broken. The orphaned child cries and surrounds her knees. The sky is hazy and merciless, the sun is bleak and discolored. The clouds are floating in the sky, and the moon is hazy and hangs on the white wall. The cold frost is zero and the swords are sharp. All the trees are shaking and the Bashan Mountains are cracking. The crows rely on their nests and their souls are frightened. Only I caress the coffin and my heart is broken. The cuckoo cries blood and the smoke is hazy. The Shu soul mourns the leaves and the grass and trees are fishy. The legacy in the ears does not disappear, and the incense of the heart vows to comfort your spirit. Therefore, Dai benefited from his mother's teachings. He understood rhyme from an early age. There is a poem inscribed on the non-American War History: I have not heard of the hardship of serving in the army, but I wish to spill hot blood on the yellow earth. With one hand, open the slave cloud, and with both wrists, strike up the revolutionary drum. At that time, he was only twelve or thirteen years old. Dai was young and had an older brother who liked to talk about science. At that time, he did not think much of his younger brother's poems.

Cold Face 163

— Ke Dingyu

The weather is divided into cold and heat. Of course, people's faces also have cold and heat differences. Strange! A good face really has warmth and heat. Friends who live in the fog at five o'clock probably don't know it. The committee members of the aesthetic society have decided to send Miss "Africa" to Hollywood.

Mysterious, anyone who has some experience in society will understand the difference between the cold and heat of people's faces.

Mr. X, who kneels on the footstool in the bedroom and cannot stand up without his wife's order, has a cold face in his office during the day, and he cannot find a trace of a smile. Even if he sees his friends, he can only hear a few sharp, cold laughs.

In the lecture hall, the teacher who holds the teaching whip and draws east and west is so majestic in front of the students. It is usually not easy to see his smile. Maybe you can see him and the female students whispering in the corner of the campus.

The office staff of the post office are really supreme positions. Look how majestic they are sitting in their positions! Especially the staff who do money orders, their cold and strange faces are often stiff. Although their hands are constantly working, the crowd of money orders outside the railing still feel that their methods are slow. When he finishes a batch of money orders, he calls out the names one by one. I think this is the time when he is proud.

In the cigarette exchange shop, they are not responsible for the copper and lead of the silver coins they exchange. If you take the silver coins exchanged from the original shop to exchange for copper coins, he will immediately slam the silver coins on the counter. After slamming them for a while, he will look at them carefully. If he doesn't tease people, he will exchange the copper coins for you. Some people will say "This is a new edition" or "Private edition". New editions and private editions are all exchanged by them. Regardless of this, if you look at his face, it is shockingly cold.

If your lover asks for something, but you are unable to cope, and you cannot get your lover's warmth, then her face must be cold, and very cold. In this coldness, there is a full of money. The remnants of love cannot be found at all.

The mediocre person who looks down on everything often prides himself on being superior, so he looks down on ordinary people. His face will have horizontal flesh. It's okay at first sight, but if you look closely, the shadows of the Ye Lang demon will wriggle in every pore of his face.

I have written several cold faces, probably quite cold. There are also prostitutes and pimps. Look at her face when she has no customers at midnight; and the fierce mistress's face towards the maid; the overbearing servant's face towards the apprentice... These faces are mostly below zero, which can be used as a summer remedy for you!

Street Psychology 164

— Zeng Shujuan

1. When you meet friends on the street, if you see them with angry faces or walking angrily, remember not to greet them, otherwise the other party will definitely respond with harsh words. Because at that time, they must have been angry with their family members at home, or quarreled with friends outside. Therefore, at that time, it is the time when they are angry and have nowhere to vent. Even if you meet them on the way, it is best not to greet them.

2. The masses on the road are usually very leisurely and relaxed; if you see people fleeing in a panic, or running wildly like angry horses, it must be a fire or trouble nearby.

3. When someone is chasing on the road, you can dodge to the side from a distance; otherwise, be careful of bullets hitting you in the face. Because most of the time, the police are chasing thieves, or the thugs are assassinating their enemies.

4. The corner is the easiest place to have an accident. Before you get there, you should use your hearing to listen for horns, shouts, or sirens from all directions, so as not to be in a dangerous place and unable to dodge.

Long Novel

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 165

— Zhang Henshui

Episode 8 Angry Words Inspire Youth to Resign and Escape, Enthusiastic Pity for Young Girl Embraces Cotton to Come

Unexpectedly, the voices of the two people talking in the outer room were getting softer and softer. They simply couldn't hear a single word. This attitude clearly indicated that the two people were keeping their words from him. Although he couldn't interfere with others, he felt very uncomfortable in his heart. Guan Yaowu talked for a long time before loudly saying goodbye and leaving. Guizhi wondered for a long time, feeling that this conversation must have something to do with him. It was late that day and there was no time to make any claims. The next day, he got up early, opened the gate and stood on the street. Seeing that the gates of Gan's house were tightly closed and had not yet opened, he thought that Ji Zhi had not gone out. He put his hands on his chest and stood against the door wall, his eyes shining like two electric lights towards the gate of Gan's house. In less than half an hour, the door opened with a creak, and Gan Ji Zhi walked out with a smile on his face. As soon as he turned his head, he saw Guizhi. However, he pretended not to know and suddenly raised the collar of his coat to cover both sides of his face, intending to walk straight away. Guizhi immediately ran after him, raising his hand and waving several times in the air, saying: Second Master Gan, Second Master Gan, are you busy? Can we talk for a few words? Ji Zhi couldn't pretend to be confused anymore, so he had to stop, turn around, and nod to him, saying: Old girl, you got up really early. Guizhi said: These days, Second Master, you go out very early and come back very late. Are you trying to avoid me? Ji Zhi laughed and said: No, no! But I'm really busy with official business. Guizhi said: Official business can't be so busy that you go early and return late. Isn't there a fixed time for doing things in the yamen? Ji Zhi laughed: But recently things have been a little busy. Guizhi didn't pursue this issue, followed behind him, and walked straight forward with him. After walking all over the streets of Haiten, Guizhi suddenly stopped and said loudly: Don't go, Second Master, I have a few words to say. Ji Zhi smiled at him and said: You didn't say anything, but you look angry first. Guizhi said: To be honest, I've been angry for a long time, but I didn't dare to express it. I heard that Second Master is afraid of losing his official position, so he doesn't dare to meet me. Is this true? (87)

Personal Anecdotes

Random Talks from Genchang 166

— Jun Ti

In the Qing Dynasty, after Confucius was ennobled as Duke Yansheng, Zhang Daoling was also ennobled as National Teacher, which was comparable. In a certain year of Guangxu, Duke Yansheng went north and Zhang Tianshi went south. They met on the Grand Canal and competed to go first, neither yielding to the other, so they moored their boats. Other boats were not allowed to pass, stretching for hundreds of miles. The governor of the Grand Canal personally came to mediate, but they would not listen, so he reported it to the emperor. The emperor ordered the Ministry of Rites to discuss it. They replied: "The Kong family does not learn the Zhang family's methods, but the Zhang family must read the Kong family's books." Therefore, the emperor ordered Duke Yansheng to go first. This was probably because the court officials favored the teacher's sake and made a one-sided statement. In fact, the Zhang family also showed that they must read the Kong family's books. Now, Duke Yansheng has already been stripped of his title, and Zhang Tianshi has also been driven out. No one reads the Kong family's books, and the Zhang family's methods have nowhere to be used. Compared with the Panchen Lama, who is uniquely ennobled, what is his luck and misfortune like!

Zuo Zongtang was a famous minister of the Qing Dynasty, known for his military skills. However, his rewards and punishments often did not follow the law. When he led his troops out of a certain place, some soldiers entered a food shop, ate noodles, and left. The shop owner did not know. Another soldier entered, took his seat, and called for noodles repeatedly. The shop owner said that he had already eaten, and would not give him any, but the soldier did not admit it. While they were arguing, Zuo arrived and immediately ordered the soldier to be killed, and his abdomen to be cut open to see his intestines and stomach. There were no noodles. Then he turned to the shop owner and said: "You made a false accusation, you should be punished." He also killed him. This is truly unheard of military law.

Han people often say that Manchus have different surnames for fathers and sons, but this is not true. According to the records, Manchus and Mongols have no surnames, but use the name of their tribe as their clan name. In peacetime, they only call their names. Assuming the person's name is Cheng Zhi, and his courtesy name is Kang Ren, then they would call him Cheng Kang Ren. If the person is a county magistrate, then they would call him Magistrate Cheng. If his son's reputation or position exceeds him, then he would also be called by the first character of his son's name, the same as the above example. Otherwise, he would be called Cheng Mou, as if Cheng were his surname. This is the origin of different surnames for fathers and sons.

In the Qing Dynasty, civil and military officials must hang a loyal and filial belt outside their robes. Its shape is roughly like an old-fashioned eyeglass case. Inside, there is a rope, a knife, and a packet of poison, which were used for赐死 or to give one's life for the country. Later, it only had a formal purpose, and it was like an ornament.

Emperor Dezong of Qing Dynasty, after experiencing hardships, had the ambition to restore clarity. He was the only wise monarch after Gaozong. Unfortunately, he had a mother like Wu Zetian and a slave like Wei Zhongxian, so he could not achieve great achievements and rival Gaozong. Is it not fate! I heard from my ancestors: "When I privately saw him when I went to court in my youth, his broad forehead and high appearance were really not mediocre. He ended up with his ambition unfulfilled, which is regrettable."

In the Qing Dynasty examinations, the county had a fixed number of quotas, so large counties often had lost talent, and small counties often filled the numbers. In small counties, there were even those who had not passed the sentence and were selected. So-and-so was also like this. I still remember the examiner's comments: "The characters are out of the ordinary, the articles are out of the question, and the poems are out of rhyme. Such a candidate is unexpected. If I do not take him, it will be an exception." It is conceivable that they must take him to meet the quota.

Peng Yualao was known in the court and the public for his integrity. In a certain year, he was sent to inspect the area. He passed through Zhenjiang and moored his boat on the river bank. Suddenly, a woman called out for help. After questioning her, she accused her adulterer of killing her husband. Previously, the woman had an affair with Bu Tou, who was favored by the county magistrate and was a tyrant. He wanted to kill her husband for a long-term plan. The woman refused, saying: "I am ashamed of having an affair with you, let alone harming him." Mou did not respond and left. After a few days, he came again and said to the woman: "Yesterday I met your husband and went to Jiao Mountain. Taking advantage of his unpreparedness, I pushed him into the river. Now I can live with you forever." The woman was terrified and said: "If so, I will accuse you." Mou smiled and said: "You can accuse me." The woman did accuse him in the county office, but it was not approved. She accused him in the prefecture, but it was not approved again. When she heard that Yualao had arrived, she presented her statement. Yualao liked to visit privately and had already learned the truth. He went to arrest Mou. At that time, the county magistrate already knew about it and was afraid that disaster would befall him. He discussed it with Mou. Mou said: "Present a sacrifice of skin and flesh, and firmly deny the truth. What can Tie Tou do to me." The county magistrate thought it was right. When he went there, he did not admit it. He was tortured, but he did not say a word, but called out for help. After repeating it several times, he still could not get a confession. Peng was angry and said: "I, the Ministry Court, will wrong you once today and kill you." The whole county cheered. Without this, it would not be enough to govern the violent and stubborn people. Peng returned and saw the emperor. Cixi said to him gently: "I heard that you killed the culprit without getting a confession. Can you guarantee that he is not wronged!" Peng replied: "Even if he is wronged, he can only blame his fate." He was especially upright for a time.

In the autocratic era, senior officials often suffered reprimands if they made mistakes. Most of the imperial decrees were issued by eunuchs. In the event of a reprimand, those who received the reprimand would bribe them heavily. Then, the eunuchs would only read "By imperial decree, reprimanded" and leave. Otherwise, they would hold the imperial decree and scold them arbitrarily, and also insult their parents. Although it was unbearable, they still had to listen respectfully. Thinking about it, it is laughable. The abuse of eunuchs can be seen here.

Talk

"Don't Discuss National Affairs" Defense 167

— I

Recently, the general group of friends wielding pens have suddenly become somewhat spirited. Everyone is unanimously shouting, "Don't discuss national affairs." It seems that in the past, they all thought national affairs could be discussed, but now they have come to a complete and profound realization that they cannot be. In reality, the world is so peaceful and the country is so enlightened that even if one wanted to discuss them, there would be nothing to discuss. It's not that it's impossible to discuss, but rather unnecessary. Frankly speaking, we have always been quite free.

Contrasting with "Don't discuss national affairs" is "Let's discuss romance," implying that only romance is worth discussing. Actually, this is also wrong. The words "romance" on the surface seem to have the leisurely and carefree connotations of "spring flowers, autumn moon" and "famous scholars' elegance." If one musters the spirit to sigh with admiration, it's indeed very romantic. Therefore, discussing romance must also have the "grand design" state of mind, and only then can it be done in such a way as to create wonderful works like "the ear hears and becomes sound, the eye sees and becomes color." And those with such a state of mind are only the likes of "mountain hermits," "lay Buddhists," "talented scholars," and "beautiful ladies." How dare we, the likes of us, presume to? If we insist on discussing it while enduring hunger and cold, then even if it doesn't come down to "one mosquito humming, two flies buzzing," we'll inevitably sigh and sing the line, "The old country is unbearable to look back upon in the bright moonlight." Inevitably, this is the sound of a fallen nation, which is again related to national affairs, and thus very dangerous.

I remember back in my middle school days, in the ancient past, it was as enlightened as it is now. However, students always loved to parade and give speeches, so the principal and the supervisors would teach us, "Don't discuss national affairs." At this time, a witty classmate posted a motto in the study, which was eight big characters: "Don't discuss national affairs, but read pornographic books." Of course, this was inevitably making trouble without reason, intentionally misinterpreting the truth of "Don't discuss national affairs." We are gentle and refined gentlemen, how could we do such a thing? However, "discussing romance" is slightly better than "reading pornographic books." Nevertheless, I always think it's neither necessary nor unnecessary.

So what should we do in these times? I think it's best to write a "biography" for Hitler, using an "immortal pen to record an immortal person." Secondly, regarding Mussolini's achievements, we can certainly write articles to promote them. And articles like "XX-ism and Love," why can't we write them? Only this is in accordance with the rules, only this is in accordance with the way of the gentleman.

Suicide and Prison in Japan 168

— Talent

The prevalence of suicide and the increase in prisons always indicate the seriousness of social ills. But what about Japan, which proclaims itself the master of maintaining peace in East Asia while denigrating China as an "unorganized country"? Recently, newspaper reports speak not only of the prevalence of suicide in Japan but also of prisons being overcrowded.

According to the Shen Bao of May 9th: "Suicides in San'en Mountain have suddenly become rampant. To date, the number of people who have jumped from the mountain to commit suicide has reached dozens. Yesterday, among the more than two thousand sightseers, there were actually six suicides... The venerable high priest of Zojo-ji Temple in Shiba will go to Oshima on the 28th to perform a grand Segaki ceremony to exorcise evil spirits."

Also, the Shen Bao of the 12th reports: "According to a survey by the Criminal Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Justice, there has been an increase of more than four thousand criminals in the past year, a rare phenomenon in recent times, and the trend is still increasing... All forty-five prisons and branch prisons across the country have reported overcrowding... The increase in urban crime is even more ferocious. The four major prisons in Tokyo and the Fukuoka prison are already unable to accommodate new prisoners..."

Observing this, we can know that the surge in suicide and crime in Japan is fierce! If this situation continues, perhaps Japan will have man-made earthquakes in addition to natural earthquakes!

In recent years, Japanese imperialism has been experiencing deepening economic panic, with small and medium-sized bourgeoisie going bankrupt one after another, and the number of unemployed laborers increasing daily. Unable to remedy the situation, they have had the wild idea of invading China as a means of saving themselves. Little do they know that the cost of launching a war of aggression against China is entirely borne by the hard-working masses. Thinking that it would save the country from economic panic, they have instead aggravated the chronic illness. The surge in suicide and crime is the inevitable result of the sharpening of economic panic.

All Kinds of Kisses 169

— Flustered Min

Mentioning the word "kiss," how sensual and nauseating! In Western countries, kissing publicly in broad daylight seems nothing rare. Chinese faces, however, are generally more tender than Western ones, and kissing has not yet reached the stage of public display. Therefore, the word "kiss" still carries some mysterious color. But there are all kinds of different ways of kissing, so let's talk about them.

Bridge Kiss

In dim sum restaurants, there are dishes called "shrimp crossing the bridge," "clear soup crossing the bridge," and so on. And in the realm of kissing, there is also a new term called "bridge kiss." What is called "crossing the bridge"? That is, when she is holding her younger brother or sister, and she and he have had some sort of emotional connection, he conveniently picks up her younger brother or sister, and gives them a big, special kiss. She thinks that this kiss has a lot of meaning in it. Therefore, after she has been kissed by him, she also kisses the child in a big way. Isn't this a "bridge kiss"?

Dry Kiss

Dry kisses are naturally not as sweet as wet kisses. For couples or lovers who are about to part ways or cannot meet each other despite being so close, they take out gifts such as photos, handkerchiefs, love letters, etc. In a clean and bright window, under the lonely lamp, when good dreams are hard to come by, tossing and turning, they cannot help but dry-kiss the treasured gifts with shyness and embarrassment. The so-called "quenching thirst by thinking of plums" and "satisfying hunger with painted cakes," the meaning of dry kisses is unexpectedly wonderful.

Flying Kiss

When eyes are flirting and two hearts are mirroring each other, sending wireless telegraphs to each other, they can only use their mouths to convey affection, flying the kiss over. If the other side returns the flying kiss, then it is a wonderful performance. What the Shanghainese call "picking up spirits" is this principle.

Stolen Kiss

Stolen kisses are the worst strategy, like cats stealing food and dogs grabbing things. If one kisses when they should not be kissing, or kisses when they do not want to kiss, and if they risk stealing a kiss, it is unlikely that they will be rewarded with a "Five Heads" beauty cigar. It is also unknown whether they will be greeted with "a thousand cuts and a rotten floating corpse." Alas. This kind of stolen kiss is both laughable and pitiful. The author is not a true devotee of kissing studies, but rather, based on what he has heard and seen in Shanghai society, there are indeed factual proofs, so he presents it to you for a bit of a joke.

Officials with wide belts and high hats fill the stone steps,

Precious treasures are specially invited to stay in grand mansions,

Page 18

The Old Villager's Heartbreaking Words 171

— Xu Zi

"The fence is broken, the wild dogs come in," these are words Mr. Buddha said last year in the "Talking Words" column of this publication. At that time, I casually glanced over them, and did not feel their pain. Now, seeing the fields and property of the Hua family being openly robbed and secretly taken, almost to the point of family ruin and death, I deeply believe that "when the family is not harmonious, outsiders will deceive." This is indeed the biggest reason for bringing about one's own financial ruin. Below are the heartbreaking words of an old villager from the Hua family:

"We," the Hua family, were originally a prominent clan, with a large population and many fields, worthy of being called a wealthy family. However, because of years of infighting among brothers, everyone only cared about selfishly competing for the inheritance. Often, it got to the point where family members did not recognize each other, and they killed each other. Although they said they were "compatriots," in reality, they treated each other like "enemies." Regarding external threats, it seemed that they were as unrelated as a horse and an ox running in different directions.

Our eastern neighbor, that local tyrant nicknamed "Dwarf Tiger," had long coveted the Hua family's many fertile fields and wanted to seize them for himself. However, the Hua family was, after all, a large clan with many brothers, and at first, he could not help but have some scruples. Ever since last year, in September, he openly occupied a large batch of fields and mountain farms in the northeastern corner belonging to the second brother. Seeing that our second young master was only busy dancing and gambling, watching as the property painstakingly built by our ancestors was robbed by the strong neighbor, he did not resist at all.

The eldest young master, on the other hand, was usually arrogant and condescending because the second young master was enjoying the legacy of his ancestors, and he did not put his eldest brother in his eyes. Now that he had lost so much property and fields, he could no longer be as spirited as before, and he could no longer "stand on equal footing" with his eldest brother. Therefore, he was happy to stand by and watch as the "Dwarf Tiger" occupied the second brother's fields.

As for the other brothers, because they each established their own households, they all held the view that "each person sweeps the snow from their own doorstep, and does not care about the frost on others' roofs." Although everyone was a compatriot, and although there was a close relationship of "when the lips are gone, the teeth are cold," they were unwilling to "work together" to "resist foreign insults."

The Dwarf Tiger saw through this weakness of the Hua family brothers, who lacked mutual assistance and unity, and he recklessly and progressively invaded the fields of the third and fourth brothers. Moreover, he committed murder, arson, rape, and robbery. The women, old, and young of the Hua family all suffered inhumane ravages. Many fine houses and villages were turned into scorched earth. Everything was desolate, wives were separated from their children, and chickens and dogs were uneasy...

The old villager sighed with tears streaming down his wrinkled face, saying: "Alas, now the Dwarf Tiger is still continuing his efforts, constantly seizing our Hua family's fields and property, and killing our old, young, men, and women. If my master's brothers do not rouse themselves and quickly catch up, and work together to resist foreign insults, then we will be 'fish on the chopping block,' and 'I will be the meat.' Thinking of the days to come, it truly makes one shiver with cold, and how can the ancestral property painstakingly built by our ancestors endure such a daily destruction? The tragedy of family ruin and death is probably imminent..."

As he said this, he fainted, sobbing uncontrollably!

Market News 172

Announcement of the Opening of the Aurora University Museum: On June 1st, according to the national calendar, from 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM, our museum will hold its opening ceremony. From that day onwards, except for Tuesdays and Sundays, the museum will be open to the public every afternoon. Our museum is the former Xujiahui Museum, founded in 1883. In 1931, it was moved to Route Lupan in the French Concession and renamed the Aurora University Museum. Our museum collects plants and animals from all over China. As for the East, countries such as Japan... One... The entire collection will be displayed for the viewers to appreciate. For example, in the mammal section, there are already hundreds of species, most of which are still being organized. Only dozens of species are displayed. The larger species include various tigers, cows, bears, leopards, whales, etc., and the smaller species include jackals, wolves, foxes, sheep, dogs, cats, etc. Due to the different places of origin, the shapes and colors vary. In the bird section, our museum... There are many birds from Jiangsu and Anhui provinces, and several species have also been collected from Fujian, Hebei, Hubei, etc., such as the bird eggs and nests owned by R.P. Savio and the Shanghai birds of M.Ch. Ggaot... are now on display in our museum. In the reptile section, only Chinese crocodiles and various turtles, tortoises, and snakes are displayed in our museum. In the fish section, our museum has very few fish, but there are about ten thousand species of mussels. Hundreds of species are also on display in the exhibition hall. In the insect section, most of the insects in our museum are collected from China, and very few are collected from abroad. Those that are available for viewing include the nests of hymenopterans and ants. In the exhibition hall, the lives of various insects are displayed, such as the nest building of wasps and bees, and the struggles between parasites and enemies. The remaining various insects will also be generally displayed in the shortest possible time for viewing. There are also ancient artifacts and treasures from ancient years. As soon as they are organized, they can be arranged for the opening. (In order to slightly limit the number of people, our museum plans to set up a ticket, each ticket costing two dimes.) Aurora University Museum.

Clerk's Communication

At the Time, I Didn't Know She Was a Married Woman 173

Editor:

I am twenty-five years old this year and have not been married. I used to be a teacher at a school in Zhabei. Because the January 28th Incident in Shanghai occurred, the school was destroyed, so I am now working as a staff member in a company. When the Sino-Japanese War broke out in Shanghai, I took refuge in a certain community center. There was a friend I had known for a while, Ms. Liang, who introduced me to a female friend named Li, who was older than me. When I met her, we were very understanding, and we developed from friendship to love, and from love to a desire to become lifelong companions. When she talked to me about marriage, I said that because my family property had been completely destroyed by the artillery fire, I had no ability to handle the marriage. She then discussed it with her mother and got her mother's consent, and then we lived together in western Shanghai. Later, due to my job, I moved to Hongkou. In January of this year, she gave birth to a daughter. Unexpectedly, last month, she suddenly told me that she was a married woman. Five years ago, she had married a husband who was doing business abroad in Hong Kong. But her husband has never returned since he left her. Her in-laws are also old-fashioned people and often quarreled over trivial matters, and she was subjected to abuse. Therefore, three years ago, she left her unhappy family and went to Guangzhou to make a living. Later, due to difficult living conditions, she moved to Shanghai, and therefore, she was introduced to me by my friend Ms. Liang. When I met her, I didn't know she was a married woman!

Sir, what can I do at this time? If I leave her now, it is pitiful that she is a lonely woman, and the child is still breastfeeding, it would be tantamount to putting them to death. How can my conscience bear to do it? If I don't leave her now, what should I do when her husband finds out? At that time, in law, what crimes should I be punished for?

Sir, what should I do now? Please guide me to a good solution!

Respectfully, Luo Ying

Editor's Note: The legal responsibility for this matter rests entirely on Ms. Li alone. Because her husband had been gone and had not returned, he violated the stipulation that "couples have the obligation to live together" and committed the crime of abandonment. In addition, she was abused by her in-laws, so she left the family. Then, when she left, she should have applied to the court for a declaration of divorce due to the absence of her husband. Later, after she met Mr. Luo and before she had a relationship with him, she should have told him the truth. Therefore, Ms. Li has the responsibility of deserting her husband and committing bigamy towards her former husband; towards Mr. Luo, she has even more responsibility for deception.

However, we must also say that the Chinese courts of today are still "grand government offices facing south, if you don't have money in your hand, don't come in." How could Ms. Li at that time have the power to apply? As for when she arrived in Shanghai, the environment was of course very difficult, and she was eager to find a man to be her pillar of support. How could she tell the truth and watch the food and clothing of a husband slip through her fingers? Therefore, from a legal point of view, despite having to bear great responsibility, we still cannot but forgive her and pity her.

Judging from the letter, Ms. Li is not an ungrateful person, otherwise, how could she have revealed the truth? Therefore, Mr. Luo seems to have no reason to break up with her now. When her husband finds out and comes to reason with her, as long as Ms. Li explains the situation, Mr. Luo can be completely free of blame. As for Ms. Li, there is no need to worry too much. In today's world, living one day is like two and a half days. When problems arise in the future, it is several times better than starving to death now. Moreover, anyone who hears of your situation will sympathize with you. Even if you end up in court, it is not difficult to seek the judge's pity and have a lenient sentence!

Fiction

The Life of the Five Concubines (Continued 24) 174

— Ling He

Twenty-one. Women and Opium

After a bout of terror, Zhang Wenbin had no intention of sleeping anymore. Although He Xiang still carefully served him to sleep, his heart was still constantly jumping. He thought, what if Minister Su had unfortunately caught me just now? Then how would I explain it? Could I have a reason to say that I stole his concubine? He is the master of the fifth madam, and Miss Liu belongs to him. So, he could not help but angrily say:

"Damn it!"

But when he thought that Miss Liu loved him passionately, and in fact, he was her possessor, he immediately felt proud and gave a wry smile.

Suddenly, footsteps sounded near his door, so he immediately closed his eyelids. It must be the fifth madam. He listened quietly. The footsteps stopped at the door for a while, then walked closer to the bed, bringing a thick fragrance of powder mixed with the scent of flesh. Then a hand reached out to cover him with the quilt, touching his cheek. So, he could no longer bear it, forcefully holding her hand, passionately kissing it, still closing his eyes and saying dreamily:

"Oh! My darling, you finally came, I was waiting for your lips."

Following these words was a burst of giggling laughter from a woman. This laughter surprised him, so he immediately opened his eyes, and could not help but be stunned. Ah, it turned out to be He Xiang blushing and smiling charmingly at him. But her charming eyes excited him, and her silent affection made him receive another kind of virgin tenderness. At this moment, he immediately sat up, violently pulled her over, sat her on his lap, and took the opportunity to tightly suck on her lips. Of course, at this time, He Xiang could not help but struggle a little, but in the end, she still went with the flow and let him enjoy himself.

Suddenly, Wu Gui shouted loudly by the stairs:

"Young Master Zhang, is Young Master Zhang there?"

He Xiang quickly climbed off the bed, tidied her hair, and walked towards Wu Gui, softly saying: "He is sleeping. What's the matter?"

"Not awake yet? The master is asking him to come over to talk."

Young Master Zhang heard clearly inside, but he had to pretend to have just woken up, and answered with a hoarse voice:

"Coming!"

Walking into the fifth madam's room, Minister Su was lying on the bed smoking. Because it was the time when he was most addicted to smoking, it was inconvenient to talk to him. He just glanced sideways and greeted him, then slowly pulled out the opium pipe and said:

"You are doing very well here, take good care of me, you know I trust you very much."

Shen Bao Local Supplement Movie Special

What Happens After They Lose Their Jobs? (Part 1) 175

— Yifan

Hollywood Affected by the Economic Collapse

Major Stars Planning for Their Own Lives

"The warmth of human kindness, the coolness of worldly affairs," is an inevitable phenomenon in societies both ancient and modern, Chinese and foreign. Take Hollywood in the United States, for example. Ever since the tide of economic collapse invaded, everyone has been rumored that Hollywood has reached the setting sun. In addition, the banks were closed for a few days, leaving the stars with nowhere to go. They wore clothes made by famous tailors, but their pockets were empty. The women's diamond-encrusted purses, besides rouge and powder puffs, had nothing else. How could these pampered and brilliant creatures live through such days? It was truly suffering all the idle air of the world! Now, it is simply better. Actually, there is a famous Hollywood female reporter named Nina Wilcox Putnam who asked the major stars an abrupt and terrible question: "If you lose your job in Hollywood, how will you live?"

That day was a banquet at the home of a major director, and this female reporter was also on the guest list. After she raised this terrible question during the banquet, the first one she attacked was Lyon Barrymore. Unprepared, he was suddenly attacked by this question. He quickly put down the salmon roe that he was about to put in his mouth, and said with wide eyes, "I can go back to the stage." "What if there are no opportunities on the stage either?" The female reporter continued to attack. Lyon Barrymore said, "Then I'm afraid I'll have to make a living by drawing." It turns out that Lyon Barrymore is a multi-talented artist. Besides movies and the stage, he is also good at pen and ink drawings and has some small fame. But this question really touched his heart, and he began to think deeply about it. After a while, he continued, "If no one buys my pen and ink drawings, I can still engage in copperplate engraving. Isn't the government always lacking good engravers? I can go to the government printing bureau. Even if I can't earn money, can't I still engrave a few for the government?" Just imagine, the famous Lyon Barrymore at that time would have to wear a magnifying glass, holding a piece of copper in one hand and a knife in the other, wearing worker's clothes, and covered in the stench of copper and the smell of strong acid. It's truly unbearable to look back on.

After the female reporter got the answer, she turned the cannon and attacked Joan Crawford again. Joan Crawford is a woman of thought. No matter what the matter is, no matter what the words are, she always thinks three times before acting and three times before speaking. She was attacked by this question, neither surprised nor laughing wildly. She calmly considered it for a while, and then said very solemnly, "I have also thought about this question from time to time. We are unfortunately born in this chaotic world, and anything is possible. As for me personally, if I stumble in the film industry, the only thing I can do is teach dancing. After I drink a cup of coffee in the morning, I will go out to various dance schools to look for a job as a dance instructor. I like teaching children to dance the most. Whether it's opening a dance class, in a school, in a theater, or in a private home, I'm willing to do it. I want to make people understand the joy of dancing well. If my luck is even worse, I can dance on the street. At that time, I'm afraid the world-famous cellist Fritz Kreisler would also be willing to play the violin for me. My love could also hold a copper basin and ask the people standing around for money." That's truly incredible! (To be continued)

Film Commentary

Review of "A Little Bitterness" 176

— Yan Nan

Sound films are developing day by day, and silent films are disappearing. This great tide has caused John Gilbert's past glory to plummet. "Living Dead" was certainly a major failure, and the public opinion of "Lower Depths" was not very good either. Although "A Little Bitterness" shown by Cathay yesterday was better than the previous two films, it still did not escape the trap of failure.

Here, he plays a worker whose companion is deceived by a wanton woman (?). Therefore, he tries his best to sabotage it, causing his companion to resent him and secretly hurt him. But in the end, the companion repents and divorces, and they are still good friends.

What is this story about? Does it represent the spirit of friendship? Does it satirize the despicable nature of gold-digging women? But it has no core. Would a gold-digging woman be fascinated by a worker with a salary of seventy-five yuan? Since the companion has resented him for a long time, would he still be willing to visit him after being injured? Obviously, there are great regrets in the script. Moreover, at the end, the companion is clearly a rejected lover, and the woman is still a wanderer. Can the responsibility of the script be considered complete with such a vague ending? The contradiction in the companion's personality before and after also reveals the imperfection of the script.

Who doesn't know that John in the silent era was a screen lover? Who doesn't admire his gentleness and beauty? Now that he is middle-aged, he doesn't have the same demeanor as before, so he has to change his style. But asking him to play a lower-class worker is really not very suitable. In fact, his pronunciation has improved a lot. The reason why he didn't succeed three times is entirely because the personality of the character in the play does not allow him to develop. Although his expression here is not particularly brilliant, it is generally very good. The scene in the hospital at the end, followed by a bitter smile, is quite touching. Robert Armstrong, who plays his companion, is too fiery. For example, after John's sabotage, his resentment is completely exposed. How capable the other party is, he makes the other party look like a foolish idiot, which is called "hard work without reward." Mae Clarke, who plays the woman, is okay. She actually did everything she should in terms of expression, vividly portraying the identity of a proud and modern woman. The remaining supporting roles are generally acceptable, but each person's individual work is limited, so there is no need to mention them.

Too many dialogues are also one of the reasons why this film is tiring. Sound recording and photography, and lighting are all around the horizontal line. Only the falling from a high building and the reunion in the hospital show the agility of the camera and the skills of dividing the scenes. The exterior scenes are very grand, and some of the interior scenes are detached from reality, not like the furnishings that should befit the identity of the characters in the play.

The director has too few interesting interjections, and he doesn't know how to use the twists and turns that a film should have to attract the audience's attention. Therefore, except for a few particularly brilliant scenes (referring to the performance and plot changes), the whole film is noticeably monotonous and boring.

For John's personal performance, the more beautiful techniques, and the neatness of the supporting actors' skills, this film may still be worth watching?

Audience Opinion

On the Sentiments of Spring Water 177

— Yu Ming

Recently, Chinese films are always calling for "changing their style," but after watching them, people can't help but be disappointed.

"Spring Water Sentiments" is the latest progressive work of the Star Film Company. It depicts all the activities under the feudal system, the ugliness of officialdom, blind love, the idea of getting promoted and making a fortune, and the darkness in patriarchal society. All of this is exposed in this film. However, the weak unity and struggle of the Northwest Reclamation Group will never break through the lives of the poor. Moreover, when it comes to overthrowing imperialism and feudal forces, this is a weakness of consciousness, which gives people a wrong idea.

Director's skills: I think it still lacks rigor. Before Tang Shusheng falls in love with Amao, a section of the initial change should be added. The scene of the lake tour, the scenery is beautiful, and the faint movements seen from the branches are very touching.

In terms of individual performances: Hu Die's expression of joy and sorrow is very considerate, but it is a pity that the expressions before and after "production" are too neglected. But from a general point of view, she is indeed very suitable to perform this character. Sun Min's performance here is very ineffective, while Yan Yuexian, Hu Ping, Wang Xianzai, and others are all competent.

In addition, the subtitles are more concise than before, but they still can't get rid of the Saturday School's writing style. Finally, I dare to say that this film is much better than the previous Free Flower and others. In Chinese films, it can be said to be not bad to have such achievements.

Thoughts After Watching "Spring Water Sentiments" 178

— Feng Ying

The giant wheel of the times has rolled into the 20th century, and the sound of love - the entity and the general young men and women - is indeed surging day by day. At the same time, newspapers are also reporting news of abandonment. If we explore with the eyes of a sociologist, we will definitely be able to analyze the cruel elements in it.

The film "Spring Water Sentiments" clearly exposes the cruelty of abandoning someone after seducing them, and the sins of gilded love. The darkness of officialdom and the meaninglessness of love are also powerfully depicted here. At the same time, it makes a powerful cry for women oppressed by feudal evil forces, especially for men who abuse love and play with women, giving them a head-on blow.

The director's methods are mediocre, which makes the plot before and after too disjointed. However, in the two scenes of the lake tour and the contrast between the sweet and bitter situations, we should not obliterate it.

In terms of actors, the most successful is Hu Die. Her performance can make the audience feel deep sympathy everywhere. Yan Yuexian is also not bad, but Sun Min feels that she has regressed compared to her previous works. Hu Ping also has considerable success.

Thoughts After Watching "Spring Water Sentiments" 179

— Xu Meilan

"Spring Water Sentiments," what a poetic title. On Sunday, there was nothing to do at school, so I went to Xin Guang with a few classmates to appreciate it.

The Star Film Company is now very concerned about women's affairs, so it has several films that discuss our women's issues. It clearly understands the environment we women are in now. It reveals everywhere how we women are being played with and how we feel sad in the current society. It exposes the ferocity of the bourgeoisie on the one hand, and the weaknesses of our women on the other. Of course, it is a good thing to use these as film themes to promote the awakening of women themselves.

Loving one and abandoning another is a common occurrence for the bourgeoisie. Naturally, they will not care about the sorrow and pain of those who are abandoned. I think in this society, women are bound to be played with and trampled on because they cannot be self-reliant and rely on men in everything. The phrase "equality between men and women" is simply deceiving. I feel that in such a bad environment, there is no other way for us women to go except to struggle. If we are not willing to live a miserable and pitiful life under the oppression of the capitalists, we must take out our perseverance and fight against the bad environment and bad society. I believe that if we can be unyielding and unyielding, victory will surely belong to us. Female compatriots, let's unite! (Chapter missing)

Thoughts After Watching "The Future" 180

— Meng Yi

What is depicted in "The Future" is a common phenomenon in modern society. Conversely, it is also a mistake that young men easily make in a society of transition between the old and the new. In passionate love, reason often cannot control emotions, so people do all kinds of self-deceiving things involuntarily. These principles are very simple and easy to understand: but the behavior of young men and women in the period of infatuation is chaotic, and the mistakes they make are often knowingly committed. In "The Future," although I do not see a little bit of cause and effect, it leaves a signpost for the general women of the times - that is: after a woman marries a husband, she cannot completely immerse herself in the river of love and rely on her husband: she must continue to work hard for her own "future."

The so-called "modern women" who are busy all day with dressing up, eating big meals, watching movies, and dancing should also wake up after watching "The Future"!

Records of Artists' Whereabouts 182

Mr. Cheng Bugao is currently directing both "Man Jiang Hong" and "Spring Silkworms," and is very busy. His work after "Spring Water Sentiments" will soon bring the old man's famous stage play "Nobleman and Prisoner" to the screen.

Mr. Cai Chusheng's long-planned new film "Fisherman's Song" is actively preparing to start shooting.

After the end of "The Future," Mr. Zhang Shichuan went to Nanchang to shoot an anti-Japanese and bandit-suppression sound film and returned to Shanghai a few days ago. His new work "The City of Prosperity" is about to start shooting, starring Ms. Xu Lai, the "Oriental Standard Beauty" who is on the screen for the first time.

An Overview of Soviet Russian Films (5) 183

— Written by Rudolf Metzl, Translated by Bao Han

In the space and time of waiting for further instructions, one can take a slight rest, whether it is one or two days, or up to a week, or after filming one film, one can continuously film other films, which are all insignificant issues, because since the beginning of his career in the film industry, he has obtained a lifelong career, but only asks that those who are engaged in the work do not change their minds and stop halfway. These employment conditions have been universally implemented throughout Soviet Russia, and are not limited to actors alone. All other people, such as carpenters, technicians, lighting engineers, and workers in the photography studio, can enjoy the same treatment.

As for the so-called movie stars, there are also movie stars in Soviet Russia, and the salary they receive is slightly comparable to that of movie stars in other countries. As for whether this special treatment of stars is in line with communist philosophy, the reader can decide for himself. However, what should be explained here is that Russian movie stars are mostly famous actors on the stage. They shoot movies during the day, are given excellent salaries, and return to various theaters at night to engage in stage life. To be promoted to a star with the qualifications of a movie lead is almost unheard of in Soviet Russia. Because the essence of Soviet Russian films is special, it is created for the application of ideas, not for the status of individuals. In addition, one thing is worth mentioning. Since the unemployment problem in Soviet Russia has been eliminated, it is impossible to temporarily hire a large number of people for a short period of time, and the film lacks crowd performance scenes. The production of modern Soviet Russian films also focuses on employing the smallest number of extras. However, when crowd performances are indispensable according to the plot, the only thing the director can do is to wait for the workers of the neighboring factories to rest, invite many people, and give each person twenty-five rubles as the price for seven hours of work. Although this method is generally convenient and feasible, it cannot be said that crowd scenes can be filmed arbitrarily in this way. Furthermore, although some workers are tempted by the twenty-five rubles and are willing to give up a day of rest, as far as the author knows, most workers would rather keep a day for recreation than get twenty-five rubles of idle money.

Furthermore, the crowds mentioned above refer to extras of more than two hundred people. As for the number of people needed in each scene being less than two hundred, all the staff of the photography studio can temporarily supplement it, such as typists, construction workers, etc., can all temporarily act as characters on the screen. However, if the number of extras required exceeds two hundred, the photography authorities have to find other ways to solicit them. (To be continued)
